-----title
礼泉（醴泉）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e26a2abbd7784d57b34ccee6cfcbd731_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e26a2abbd7784d57b34ccee6cfcbd731");'><span id='e26a2abbd7784d57b34ccee6cfcbd731_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>，15岁</div><div id='e26a2abbd7784d57b34ccee6cfcbd731' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　至醴泉。十年后再到。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='509ca03051114f03b498284d02ed72e1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("509ca03051114f03b498284d02ed72e1");'><span id='509ca03051114f03b498284d02ed72e1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年</a>，59岁</div><div id='509ca03051114f03b498284d02ed72e1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年</a>　至关中，改葬程俶。作品：改葬告少监文。<div id='poem_1183792' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183792' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183792?labeling=true' target='_blank'>改葬告少监文</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐六年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183792")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183792_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183792'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183792'>维元祐六年辛未二月癸卯，玄孙右承议郎、权司管勾西京国子监、轻车都尉、赐绯鱼袋珫，谨遣侄颐就坟所，以酒肴之具，祭告于高祖少监、高祖母京兆太君段氏之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183792_comment'></div>秦人之俗，以开发冢墓为事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183792_comment'></div>近年以来，大评事、四评事墓继遭盗劫，少师墓亦尝有穴，固不知完否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183792_comment'></div>茍不完矣，理当改厝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183792_comment'></div>幸而尚完，异日之祸，不得不虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183792_comment'></div>今将改葬少师，而迁公丘封，使后人不知墓之所在，以图永安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183792_comment'></div>谨具昭告，伏惟鉴飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1183792_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南京
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e89f09bf1f624f3f9c92cc63be07472d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e89f09bf1f624f3f9c92cc63be07472d");'><span id='e89f09bf1f624f3f9c92cc63be07472d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1054')">1052-1054年</a>，20-22岁</div><div id='e89f09bf1f624f3f9c92cc63be07472d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年2月28日</a>　随父居江宁。母亲侯夫人卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　开始解释经义，研读《春秋》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　随父居江宁。母亲侯夫人卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　随父居江宁，作《养鱼记》<div id='poem_1183767' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183767' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183767?labeling=true' target='_blank'>养鱼记<span class='inlineComment2'>（时年二十二）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183767")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183767_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183767'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183767'>书斋之前有石盆池，家人买鱼子食猫，见其煦沫也，不忍，因择可生者，得百馀，养其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183767_comment'></div>大者如指，细者如箸，支颐而观之者竟日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183767_comment'></div>始舍之，洋洋然，鱼之得其所也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183767_comment'></div>终观之，戚戚焉，吾之感于中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183767_comment'></div>吾读古圣人书，观古圣人之政，禁数罟不得入洿池，鱼尾不盈尺不中杀，市不得鬻，人不得食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183767_comment'></div>圣人之仁，养物而不伤也如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183767_comment'></div>物获如是，则吾人之乐其生，遂其性，宜何如哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183767_comment'></div>思是鱼之于是时，宁有是困耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183767_comment'></div>推是鱼，孰不可见耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183767_comment'></div>鱼乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183767_comment'></div>鱼乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183767_comment'></div>细钩密网，吾不得禁之于彼，炮燔咀嚼，吾得免尔于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183767_comment'></div>吾知江海之大，足使尔遂其性，思置汝于彼，而未得其路，徒能以斗斛之水，生汝之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183767_comment'></div>生汝诚吾心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183767_comment'></div>汝得生已多，万类天地中，吾心将奈何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183767_comment'></div>鱼乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183767_comment'></div>鱼乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183767_comment'></div>感吾心之戚戚者，岂止鱼而已乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183767_comment'></div>因作《养鱼记》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183767_comment'></div>至和甲午季夏记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1183767_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
开封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e769ba714c3c41278a0750479cca3254_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e769ba714c3c41278a0750479cca3254");'><span id='e769ba714c3c41278a0750479cca3254_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1057')">1056-1057年</a>，24-25岁</div><div id='e769ba714c3c41278a0750479cca3254' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　至京师，始居河南。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　在京师游太学，胡瑗以《颜子所好何学论》试诸生，得到胡瑗赏识。吕原明首师事之，继而授徒讲学。过邑拜访少师。<div id='poem_1183745' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183745' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183745?labeling=true' target='_blank'>颜子所好何学论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183745")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183745_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183745'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183745'>圣人之门，其徒三千，独称颜子为好学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183745_comment'></div>夫《诗》、《书》六艺，三千子非不习而通也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183745_comment'></div>然则颜子所独好者，何学也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183745_comment'></div>学以至圣人之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183745_comment'></div>圣人可学而至欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183745_comment'></div>曰：然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183745_comment'></div>学之道如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183745_comment'></div>曰：天地储精，得五行之秀者为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183745_comment'></div>其本也真而静，其未发也五性具焉，曰仁、义、礼、智、信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183745_comment'></div>形既生矣，外物触其形而动于中矣，其中动而七情出焉，曰喜、怒、哀、乐、爱、恶、欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183745_comment'></div>情既炽而益荡，其性凿矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183745_comment'></div>是故觉者约其情使合于中，正其心，养其性，故曰性其情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183745_comment'></div>愚者则不知制之，纵其情而至于邪僻，梏其性而亡之，故曰情其性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183745_comment'></div>凡学之道，正其心，养其性而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183745_comment'></div>中正而诚，则圣矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183745_comment'></div>君子之学，必先明诸心，知所养，然后力行以求至，所谓自明而诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183745_comment'></div>故学必尽其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183745_comment'></div>尽其心，则知其性，知其性，反而诚之，圣人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183745_comment'></div>故《洪范》曰：「思曰睿，睿作圣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183745_comment'></div>诚之之道，在乎信道笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1183745_comment'></div>信道笃则行之果，行之果则守之固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1183745_comment'></div>仁义忠信不离乎心，造次必于是，颠沛必于是，出处语默必于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1183745_comment'></div>久而弗失，则居之安，动容周旋中礼，而邪僻之心无自生矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1183745_comment'></div>故颜子所事，则曰「非礼勿视，非礼勿听，非礼勿言，非礼勿动」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1183745_comment'></div>仲尼称之，则曰「得一善，则拳拳服膺而弗失之矣」，又曰「不迁怒，不贰过，有不善未尝不知，知之未尝复行也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1183745_comment'></div>此其好之笃学之之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1183745_comment'></div>视听言动皆礼矣，所异于圣人者，盖圣人则不思而得，不勉而中，从容中道，颜子则必思而后得，必勉而后中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1183745_comment'></div>故曰：颜子之与圣人，相去一息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1183745_comment'></div>孟子曰：「充实而有光辉之谓大，大而化之之谓圣，圣而不可知之谓神」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1183745_comment'></div>颜子之德，可谓充实而有光辉矣，所未至者，守之也，非化之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1183745_comment'></div>以其好学之心，假之以年，则不日而化矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1183745_comment'></div>故仲尼曰：「不幸短命死矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1183745_comment'></div>盖伤其不得至于圣人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1183745_comment'></div>所谓化之者，入于神而自然不思而得，不勉而中之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1183745_comment'></div>孔子曰「七十而从心所欲不踰矩」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1183745_comment'></div>或曰：「圣人，生而知之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1183745_comment'></div>今谓可学而至，其有稽乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1183745_comment'></div>曰：「然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1183745_comment'></div>孟子曰：『尧、舜性之也，汤、武反之也』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1183745_comment'></div>性之者，生而知之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1183745_comment'></div>反之者，学而知之者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1183745_comment'></div>又曰：「孔子则生而知也，孟子则学而知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1183745_comment'></div>后人不达，以谓圣本生知，非学可至，而为学之道遂失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1183745_comment'></div>不求诸己而求诸外，以博闻强记、巧文丽辞为工，荣华其言，鲜有至于道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1183745_comment'></div>则今之学，与颜子所好异矣」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1183745_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　在京师，吕希哲首师事之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　与方元采手帖。<div id='poem_1183727' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183727' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183727?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与方元寀手帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183727")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183727_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183727'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183727'>圣人之道，坦如大路，学者病不得其门耳，得其门，无远之不可到也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183727_comment'></div>求入其门，不由于经乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183727_comment'></div>今之治经者亦众矣，然而买椟还珠之蔽，人人皆是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183727_comment'></div>经所以载道也，诵其言辞，解其训诂，而不及道，乃无用之糟粕耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183727_comment'></div>觊足下由经以求道，勉之又勉，异日见卓尔有立于前，然后不知手之舞，足之蹈，不加勉而不能自止矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1183727_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='43b0af61165e4422a497ca0649161c35_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("43b0af61165e4422a497ca0649161c35");'><span id='43b0af61165e4422a497ca0649161c35_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1066')">1059-1066年</a>，27-34岁</div><div id='43b0af61165e4422a497ca0649161c35' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　举进士不中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　叔父程瑜卒于京师。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　吕公著请为太学正，固辞。作品：谢吕晦叔待制相见书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年4月</a>　诏议崇奉濮王典礼，代彭中丞论濮王称亲疏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年8月</a>　京师大水，应诏上书。作品：代其父程珦应诏上书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年9月</a>　吕公著知蔡州临行举荐程颐，程颐自以为学不足不愿仕。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='074d410ac48047a6a4b24c0d532023cf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("074d410ac48047a6a4b24c0d532023cf");'><span id='074d410ac48047a6a4b24c0d532023cf_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1088')">1086-1088年</a>，54-56岁</div><div id='074d410ac48047a6a4b24c0d532023cf' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年2月</a>　朱光庭奏乞以程颐为讲官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年闰2月24日</a>　除秘书省校书郎，辞免。作品：辞免馆职状。<div id='poem_1183660' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183660' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183660?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免馆职状<span class='inlineComment2'>（元祐元年闰二月二十四日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年闰2月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183660")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183660_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183660'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183660'>伏蒙圣恩，授臣宣德郎，秘书省校书郎，闻命震惊，不知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183660_comment'></div>臣昨蒙恩，授西京国子监教授，方再具辞免，奉圣旨，令乘递马赴阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183660_comment'></div>祗命而来，未获进见，遽然有此除授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183660_comment'></div>伏念臣草莱之人，既蒙赐召，礼合见君，先受恩命，义理未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183660_comment'></div>况祖宗朝布衣被召者，故事具存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183660_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，令臣入见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183660_comment'></div>所降诰命，不敢当受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183660_comment'></div>伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1183660_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　王岩叟荐程颐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　上书论经筵事。作品：论经筵第一劄子。论经筵第二劄子。论经筵第三劄子。<div id='poem_1183662' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183662' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183662?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论经筵第一劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年3月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183662")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183662_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183662'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183662'>臣伏观自古人君守成而致盛治者，莫如周成王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183662_comment'></div>成王之所以成德，由周公之辅养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183662_comment'></div>昔者周公辅成王，幼而习之，所见必正事，所闻必正言，左右前后皆正人，故习与智长，化与心成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183662_comment'></div>今士大夫家善教子弟者，亦必延名德端方之士，与之居处，使之薰染成性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183662_comment'></div>故曰：「少成若天性，习惯如自然」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183662_comment'></div>伏以皇帝陛下春秋之富，虽睿圣之资得于天禀，而辅养之道不可不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183662_comment'></div>所谓辅养之道，非谓告诏以言，过而后谏也，在涵养薰陶而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183662_comment'></div>大率一日之中，亲贤士大夫之时多，亲寺人宫女之时少，则自然气质变化，德器成就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183662_comment'></div>欲乞朝廷慎选贤德之士，以侍劝讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183662_comment'></div>讲读既罢，常留二人直日，夜则一人直宿，以备访问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183662_comment'></div>皇帝习读之暇，游息之閒，时于内殿召见，从容宴语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183662_comment'></div>不独渐磨道义，至于人情物态，稼穑艰难，积久自然通达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183662_comment'></div>比之常在深宫之中，为益岂不甚大？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183662_comment'></div>窃闻间日一开经筵，讲读数行，群官列侍，俨然而退，情意略不相接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183662_comment'></div>如此而责辅养之功，不亦难乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183662_comment'></div>今主上冲幼，太皇太后慈爱，亦未敢便乞频出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183662_comment'></div>但时见讲官，久则自然接熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183662_comment'></div>大抵与近习处久熟则生亵慢，与贤士大夫处久熟则生爱敬，此所以养成圣德，为宗社生灵之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183662_comment'></div>天下之事，无急于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183662_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1183662_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1183662'>〔贴黄〕臣窃料众人之意，必以为皇帝尚幼，未烦如此，此乃浅近之见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1183662_comment'></div>夫幼而习之，为功则易；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1183662_comment'></div>发然后禁，礼经所非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1183662_comment'></div>古人所以自能食能言而教者，盖为此也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1183662_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1183663' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183663' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183663?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论经筵第二劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183663")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183663_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183663'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183663'>臣闻三代之时，人君必有师傅保之官：师，道之教训；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183663_comment'></div>傅，傅其德义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183663_comment'></div>保，保其身体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183663_comment'></div>后世作事无本，知求治而不知正君，知规过而不知养德，傅德义之道固已疏矣，保身体之法复无闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183663_comment'></div>伏惟太皇太后陛下聪明睿哲，超越前古，皇帝陛下春秋之富，辅养之道，当法先王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183663_comment'></div>臣以为傅德义者，在乎防见闻之非，节嗜好之过；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183663_comment'></div>保其体者，在乎适起居之宜，存畏慎之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183663_comment'></div>臣欲乞皇帝左右扶侍祗应宫人内臣，并选年四十五已上，厚重小心之人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183663_comment'></div>服用器玩皆须质朴，一应华巧奢丽之物，不得至于上前；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183663_comment'></div>要在侈靡之物不接于目，浅俗之言不入于耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183663_comment'></div>及乞择内臣十人，充经筵祗应，以伺候皇帝起居，凡动息必使经筵官知之，有剪桐之戏则随事箴规，违持养之方则应时谏止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183663_comment'></div>调护圣躬，莫过于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183663_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183663_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1183663'>〔贴黄〕今不设保傅之官，傅德义、保身体之责皆在经筵，皇帝在宫中语言动作衣服饮食，皆当使经筵官知之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1183663_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1183664' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183664' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183664?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论经筵第三劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183664")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183664_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183664'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183664'>臣窃以人主居崇高之位，持威福之柄，百官畏惧，莫敢仰视，万方承奉，所欲随得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183664_comment'></div>茍非知道畏义，所养如此，其惑可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183664_comment'></div>中常之君，无不骄肆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183664_comment'></div>英明之主，自然满假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183664_comment'></div>此自古同患，治乱所系也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183664_comment'></div>故周公告成王，称前王之德，以寅畏祗惧为首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183664_comment'></div>从古以来，未有不尊贤畏相而能成其圣者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183664_comment'></div>皇帝陛下未亲庶政，方专问学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183664_comment'></div>臣以为辅养圣德，莫先寅恭，动容周旋，当主于此，岁月积习，自成圣性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183664_comment'></div>臣窃闻经筵臣寮侍者皆坐，而讲者独立，于礼为悖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183664_comment'></div>欲乞今后特令坐讲，不惟义理为顺，所以养主上尊儒重道之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183664_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183664_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1183664'>〔贴黄〕窃闻讲官在御案旁，以手指书，所以不坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183664_comment'></div>欲乞别一人指书，讲官稍远御案坐讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183664_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1183664'>〔贴黄〕臣窃意朝廷循沿旧体，只以经筵为一美事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183664_comment'></div>臣以为，天下重任，唯宰相与经筵：天下治乱系宰相，君德成就责经筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183664_comment'></div>由此言之，安得不以为重？</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1183664_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年3月24日</a>　充崇政殿说书。作品：辞免崇政殿说书表。再辞免状。<div id='poem_1183665' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183665' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183665?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免崇政殿说书表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年3月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183665")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183665_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183665'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183665'>臣颐言：准閤门告报，伏蒙圣恩，除臣通直郎，充崇政殿说书者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183665_comment'></div>臣昨上殿，面奉德音，已尝沥恳辞避；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183665_comment'></div>及继有陈奏，愚诚已竭，天听不回<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183665_comment'></div>窃以儒者得以经术进说于人主之前，言信则志行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183665_comment'></div>自昔抱道之士，孰不愿之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183665_comment'></div>顾恨弗获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183665_comment'></div>臣何人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183665_comment'></div>有此遭遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183665_comment'></div>然臣窃观前古君臣道合，靡不由至诚感动，信以发志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183665_comment'></div>今臣道未行于家室，善未信于乡党，何足以感动人主之心乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183665_comment'></div>苟不度其诚之未至，而欲善辞说于进对之间，为一时之观则可矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183665_comment'></div>必欲通于神明，光于四海，久诚而无斁，臣知其不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183665_comment'></div>臣是以欲进而思义，喜时而愧己，冒犯天威，而尽其区区之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183665_comment'></div>伏以皇帝陛下春秋之富，方赖左右前后之人辅养圣性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183665_comment'></div>劝讲之职，任莫重焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183665_comment'></div>窃惟海宇之广，贤俊至多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183665_comment'></div>臣愿朝廷博谋群臣，旁加收择，期得出类之贤，寘诸左右，辅成圣德，为庙社生灵之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183665_comment'></div>如臣之愚，实惧不足以当重任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183665_comment'></div>所有诰命，不敢当受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183665_comment'></div>谨奉表辞免以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1183665_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年4月</a>　乞命讲官以六参日上殿问起居。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年5月12日</a>　命同修学制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　在京师，有启谢韩绛。作品：谢韩康公启。<div id='poem_1183708' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183708' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183708?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢韩康公启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183708")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183708_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183708'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183708'>窃以朝廷取士，所以为致治之先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183708_comment'></div>公卿荐贤，固必有知人之哲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183708_comment'></div>允谐公议，始厌众闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183708_comment'></div>颐也不才，少而从学，致知格物，粗窥圣道之端倪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183708_comment'></div>明善诚身，未得古人之髣髴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183708_comment'></div>徒忘怀于白首，窃有志于斯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183708_comment'></div>时和岁丰，已足素望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183708_comment'></div>言扬德进，敢有觊心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183708_comment'></div>属嗣皇访落之初，乃元老告猷之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183708_comment'></div>岂虞过听，猥被明扬？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183708_comment'></div>文陛进登，被德音之温厚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183708_comment'></div>西清入侍，密宸扆之光辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183708_comment'></div>考于近世以来，可谓非常之遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183708_comment'></div>荷恩为愧，揣分则逾，若何行为，可以报称？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183708_comment'></div>惟殚素学，勉副厚知，过此以还，不知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183708_comment'></div>末缘望履，徒切向风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183708_comment'></div>悃愊所怀，敷宣罔既。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1183708_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　在京师，有书信谢韩绛。作品：谢韩康公简。<div id='poem_1183709' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183709' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183709?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢韩康公小简</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183709")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183709_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183709'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183709'>颐惶恐再拜启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183709_comment'></div>仲夏毒热，伏惟台候动止万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183709_comment'></div>颐执耕畎亩，于门下未尝有一日之素，猥蒙过听，荐之于朝，沾被恩命，何以称报？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183709_comment'></div>末由展觌，伏冀上为宗社，善护寝兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183709_comment'></div>下情区区之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1183709_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　在京师，与吕大忠有书信往来。作品：答吕进伯简。<div id='poem_1183710' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183710' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183710?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答吕进伯简三</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183710")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183710_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183710'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183710'>相别累年，区区企渴之深，言不尽意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183710_comment'></div>按部往来，想亦劳止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183710_comment'></div>秦人疮瘵未复，而偶此旱暵，赖贤使者措置，受赐何涯！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183710_comment'></div>儒者逢时，生灵之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183710_comment'></div>勉成休功，乃所愿望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183710_comment'></div>颐备员于此，夙夜自竭，未见其补，时望赐书，开谕不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183710_comment'></div>与叔每过从，至慰至幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183710_comment'></div>引傃门墙，坐驰神爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183710_comment'></div>所欲道者，非面不尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183710_comment'></div>惟千万自爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183710_comment'></div>别纸见谕，持法为要，其来已久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183710_comment'></div>既为今日官，当于今日事中，图所设施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183710_comment'></div>旧法之拘，不得有为者，举世皆是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183710_comment'></div>以颐观之，茍迁就于法中，所可为者尚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183710_comment'></div>先兄明道之为邑，及民之事多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183710_comment'></div>众人所谓法所拘者，然为之未尝大戾于法，众亦不甚骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183710_comment'></div>谓之得伸其志则不可，求小补，则过今之为政者远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183710_comment'></div>人虽异之，不至指为狂也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183710_comment'></div>至谓之狂，则大骇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183710_comment'></div>尽诚为之，不容而后去，又何嫌乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1183710_comment'></div>鄙见如此，进伯以为如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1183710_comment'></div>荷公知遇之厚，辄有少见，上补聪明，亦久怀愤郁，无所控告，遇公而伸尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1183710_comment'></div>王者父天母地，昭事之道，当极严恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1183710_comment'></div>汉武远祀地祇于汾脽，既为非礼，后世复建祠宇，其失已甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1183710_comment'></div>因唐妖人作《韦安道传》，遂为塑像以配食，诬渎天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1183710_comment'></div>天下之妄，天下之恶，有大于此者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1183710_comment'></div>公为使者，此而不正，将正何事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1183710_comment'></div>愿以其像投之河流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1183710_comment'></div>慎勿先露，先露则传骇观听矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1183710_comment'></div>勿请勿议，必见沮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1183710_comment'></div>毋虞后患，典宪不能相及，亦可料也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1183710_comment'></div>愿公勿疑。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1183710_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　在京师，有书信与吕大临讨论“中”作品：与吕太临论中书。<div id='poem_1183711' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183711' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183711?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与吕大临论中书<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183711")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183711_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1183711_0'>① 此书其全不可复见，今只据吕氏所录到者编之。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183711'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183711'>大临云：中者道之所由出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183711_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1183711'>先生曰：中者道之所由出，此语有病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183711_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1183711'>大临云：谓中者道之所由出，此语有病，已悉所谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183711_comment'></div>但论其所同，不容更有二名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183711_comment'></div>别而言之，亦不可混为一事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183711_comment'></div>如所谓「天命之谓性，率性之谓道」，又曰「中者天下之大本，和者天下之达道」，则性与道，大本与达道，岂有二乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183711_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1183711'>先生曰：中即道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183711_comment'></div>若谓道出于中，则道在中外，别为一物矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183711_comment'></div>所谓「论其所同，不容更有二名，别而言之，亦不可混为一事」，此语固无病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183711_comment'></div>若谓性与道，大本与达道，可混而为一，即未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183711_comment'></div>在天曰命，在人曰性，循性曰道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183711_comment'></div>性也，命也，道也，各有所当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183711_comment'></div>大本言其体，达道言其用，体用自殊，安得不为二乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183711_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1183711'>大临云：既云「率性之谓道」，则循性而行莫非道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183711_comment'></div>此非性中别有道也，中即性也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183711_comment'></div>在天为命，在人为性，由中而出者莫非道，所以言道之所由出也，与「率性之谓道」之义同，亦非道中别有中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183711_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1183711'>先生曰：「中即性也」，此语极未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183711_comment'></div>中也者，所以状性之体段<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183711_comment'></div>如称天圆地方，遂谓方圆即天地，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183711_comment'></div>方圆既不可谓之天地，则万物决非方圆之所出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1183711_comment'></div>如中既不可谓之性，则道何从称出于中？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1183711_comment'></div>盖中之为义，无过不及而立名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1183711_comment'></div>若只以中为性，则中与性不合，与「率性之谓道」其义自异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1183711_comment'></div>性道不可合一而言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1183711_comment'></div>中止可言体，而不可与性同德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1183711_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1183711'>又曰：观此义，谓不可与性同德，字亦未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1183711_comment'></div>子居对以中者性之德，却为近之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1183711_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1183711'>又曰：不偏之谓中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1183711_comment'></div>道无不中，故以中形道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1183711_comment'></div>若谓道出于中，则天圆地方，谓方圆者天地所自出，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1183711_comment'></div>大临云：不倚之谓中，不杂之谓和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1183711_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1183711'>先生曰：不倚之谓中，甚善<span class='inlineComment2'>（语犹未莹）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1183711_comment'></div>不杂之谓和，未当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1183711_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1183711'>大临云：喜怒哀乐之未发，则赤子之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1183711_comment'></div>当其未发，此心至虚，无所偏倚，故谓之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1183711_comment'></div>以此心应万物之变，无往而非中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1183711_comment'></div>孟子曰：「权然后知轻重，度然后知长短，物皆然，心为甚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1183711_comment'></div>此心度物，所以甚于权衡之审者，正以至虚无所偏倚故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1183711_comment'></div>有一物存乎其閒，则轻重长短皆失其中矣，又安得如权如度乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1183711_comment'></div>故大人不失其赤子之心，乃所谓允执其中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1183711_comment'></div>大临始者有见于此，便指此心名为中，故前言中者道之所由出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1183711_comment'></div>今细思之，乃命名未当尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1183711_comment'></div>此心之状，可以言中，未可便指此心名之曰中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1183711_comment'></div>所谓以中形道，正此意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1183711_comment'></div>「率性之谓道」者，循性而行，无往而非理义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1183711_comment'></div>以此心应万事之变，亦无往而非理义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1183711_comment'></div>皆非指道体而言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1183711_comment'></div>若论道体，又安可言由中而出乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1183711_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_1183711'>先生曰：喜怒哀乐未发谓之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1183711_comment'></div>赤子之心，发而未远于中，若便谓之中，是不识大本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1183711_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_1183711'>大临云：圣人智周万物，赤子全未有知，其心固有不同矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1183711_comment'></div>然推孟子所云，岂非止取纯一无伪，可与圣人同乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1183711_comment'></div>非谓无毫发之异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1183711_comment'></div>大临前日所云，亦取诸此而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1183711_comment'></div>此义，大临昔者既闻先生君子之教，反求诸己，若有所自得，参之前言往行，将无所不合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1183711_comment'></div>由是而之焉，似得其所安，以是自信不疑，拳拳服膺，不敢失坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1183711_comment'></div>今承教，乃云已失大本，茫然不知所向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1183711_comment'></div>窃恐辞命不明，言不逮意，致高明或未深喻，辄露所见，求益左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1183711_comment'></div>卒为赐教，指其迷谬，幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1183711_comment'></div>圣人之学，以中为大本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1183711_comment'></div>虽尧、舜相授以天下，亦云「允执其中」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1183711_comment'></div>中者，无过不及之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1183711_comment'></div>何所准则而知过不及乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1183711_comment'></div>求之此心而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1183711_comment'></div>此心之动，出入无时，何从而守之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1183711_comment'></div>求之于喜怒哀乐未发之际而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1183711_comment'></div>当是时也，此心即赤子之心<span class='inlineComment2'>（纯一无伪）</span>，即天地之心<span class='inlineComment2'>（神明不测）</span>，即孔子之「绝四<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>」，即孟子所谓「物皆然，心为甚<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>」，即《易》所谓「寂然不动，感而遂通天下之故」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1183711_comment'></div>此心所发，纯是义理，与天下之所同然，安得不和？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1183711_comment'></div>大临前日敢指赤子之心为中者，其说如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1183711_comment'></div>来教云：「赤子之心可谓之和，不可谓之中」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1183711_comment'></div>大临思之，所谓和者，指已发而言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1183711_comment'></div>今言赤子之心，乃论其未发之际，纯一无伪，无所偏倚，可以言中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1183711_comment'></div>若谓已发，恐不可言心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1183711_comment'></div>来教云：「所谓循性而行，无往而非理义，言虽无病，而圣人气味殊少」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1183711_comment'></div>大临反而思之，方觉辞气迫窘，无沈浸醲厚之风，此则浅陋之罪，敢不承教？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1183711_comment'></div>大临更不敢拜书先生左右，恐烦枉答，只令义山持此请教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1183711_comment'></div>蒙塞未达，不免再三浼渎，惟望乘閒口谕义山，传诲一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1183711_comment'></div>幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1183711_comment'></div>幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1183711_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_79_1183711'>先生曰：所云非谓无毫发之异，是有异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1183711_comment'></div>有异者得为大本乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1183711_comment'></div>推此一言，馀皆可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1183711_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_82_1183711'>大临云：大临以赤子之心为未发，先生以赤子之心为已发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1183711_comment'></div>所谓大本之实，则先生与大临之言，未有异也，但解赤子之心一句不同尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1183711_comment'></div>大临初谓赤子之心，正取纯一无伪，与圣人同，恐孟子之义亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1183711_comment'></div>更不曲折一一较其同异，故指以为言，固未尝以已发不同处为大本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1183711_comment'></div>先生谓凡言心者，皆指已发而言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1183711_comment'></div>然则未发之前，谓之无心可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1183711_comment'></div>窃谓未发之前，心体昭昭具在，已发乃心之用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1183711_comment'></div>此所深疑未喻，又恐传言者失指，切望指教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1183711_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_90_1183711'>先生曰：所论意，虽以已发者为未发；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1183711_comment'></div>反求诸言，却是认已发者为说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1183711_comment'></div>词之未莹，乃是择之未精尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1183711_comment'></div>凡言心者，指已发而言，此固未当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1183711_comment'></div>心一也，有指体而言者<span class='inlineComment2'>（寂然不动是也。）</span>，有指用而言者<span class='inlineComment2'>（感而遂通天下之故是也。）</span>，惟观其所见如何耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1183711_comment'></div>大抵论愈精微，言愈易差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1183711_comment'></div>所谓传言者失指，及反覆观之，虽曰有差，亦不失大意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1183711_comment'></div>又如前论「中即性也」，已是分而为二，不若谓之性中<span class='inlineComment2'>（性中语未甚莹。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1183711_comment'></div>以谓圣人气味殊少，亦不须言圣人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1183711_comment'></div>第二书所答去者，极分明矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_99_1183711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1183711'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_17_1183711_0'>⑴ 若谓性有体段亦不可，姑假此以明彼。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_66_1183711_2'>⑵ 四者有一物存乎其间，则不得其中。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_66_1183711_1'>⑶ 心无偏倚，则至明至平，其察物甚于权度之审。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1183711_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　在京师，苏季明问“中”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年6月</a>　上疏高太后论辅养君德。作品：上太皇太后书。<div id='poem_1183668' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183668' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183668?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上太皇太后书</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183668")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183668_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183668'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183668'>六月日，具位臣程颐，昧死再拜上书太皇太后陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183668_comment'></div>臣愚鄙之人，自少不喜进取，以读书求道为事，于兹几三十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183668_comment'></div>当英祖朝暨神宗之初，屡为当涂者称荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183668_comment'></div>臣于斯时，自顾学之不足，不愿仕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183668_comment'></div>及皇帝陛下嗣位，太皇太后陛下临朝，求贤愿治，大臣上体圣意，搜扬岩穴，首及微贱，蒙恩除西京学官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183668_comment'></div>臣于斯时，未有意于仕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183668_comment'></div>辞避方再，而遽有召命，臣门下学者，促臣行者半，劝臣勿行者半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183668_comment'></div>促臣行者则曰：「君命召，礼不俟驾」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183668_comment'></div>劝臣勿行者则曰：「古之儒者，召之则不往」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183668_comment'></div>臣以为召而不往，惟子思、孟轲则可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183668_comment'></div>盖二人者，处宾师之位，不往所以规其君也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183668_comment'></div>己之微贱，食土之毛而为王民，召而不至，邦有常宪，是以奔走应命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183668_comment'></div>到阙，蒙恩授馆职，方以义辞，遂蒙召对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183668_comment'></div>臣于斯时，尚未有意于仕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183668_comment'></div>进至帘前，咫尺天光，未尝敢以一言及朝政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183668_comment'></div>陛下视臣，岂求进者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183668_comment'></div>既而亲奉德音，擢至经筵，事出望外，惘然警惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183668_comment'></div>臣窃内思，儒者得以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1183668", 1183668, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>道学</span>辅人主，盖非常之遇，使臣自择所处，亦无过于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183668_comment'></div>臣于斯时，虽以不才而辞，然许国之心，实已萌矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183668_comment'></div>尚虑陛下贪贤乐善，果于取人，知之或未审也，故又进其狂言，以觊详察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1183668_comment'></div>如小有可用，则敢不就职？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1183668_comment'></div>或狂妄无取，则乞听辞避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1183668_comment'></div>章再上，再命祗受，是陛下不以为妄也，臣于是受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1183668_comment'></div>供职而来，夙夜毕精竭虑，惟欲主上德如尧、舜，异日天下享尧、舜之治，庙社固无穷之基，乃臣之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1183668_comment'></div>臣本山野之人，禀性朴直，言辞鄙拙，则有之矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1183668_comment'></div>至于爱君之心，事君之礼，告君之道，敢有不尽？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1183668_comment'></div>上赖圣明，可以昭鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1183668_comment'></div>臣自惟至愚，蒙陛下特达之知，遭遇如此，愿效区区之诚，庶几毫发之补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1183668_comment'></div>惟陛下留意省览，不胜幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1183668_comment'></div>伏以太皇太后陛下，心存至公，躬行大道，开纳忠言，委用耆德，不止维持大业，且欲兴致太平，前代英主所不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1183668_comment'></div>但能日慎一日，天下之事不足虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1183668_comment'></div>臣以为今日至大至急，为宗社生灵久长之计，惟是辅养上德而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1183668_comment'></div>历观前古，辅养幼主之道，莫备于周公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1183668_comment'></div>周公之为，万世之法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1183668_comment'></div>臣愿陛下扩高世之见，以圣人之言为可必信，先王之道为可必行，勿狃滞于近规，勿迁惑于众口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1183668_comment'></div>古人所谓周公，岂欺我哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1183668_comment'></div>周公作《立政》之书，举言常伯，至于缀衣虎贲，以为知恤兹者鲜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1183668_comment'></div>一篇之中，丁宁重复，惟在此一事而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1183668_comment'></div>又曰「仆臣正，厥后克正」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1183668_comment'></div>又曰「后德惟臣，不德惟臣」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1183668_comment'></div>又曰「侍御仆从，罔匪正人，以旦夕承弼厥辟，出入起居，罔有不钦」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1183668_comment'></div>是古人之意，人主跬步不可离正人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1183668_comment'></div>盖所以涵养气质，薰陶德性，故能习与智长，化与心成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1183668_comment'></div>后世不复知此，以为人主就学，所以涉书史，览古今也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1183668_comment'></div>不知涉书史，览古今，乃一端尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1183668_comment'></div>若止于如是，则能文宫人可以备劝讲，知书内侍可以充辅导，何用置官设职，精求贤德哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1183668_comment'></div>大抵人主受天之命，禀赋自殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1183668_comment'></div>历考前史，帝王才质，鲜不过人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1183668_comment'></div>然而完德有道之君至少，其故何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1183668_comment'></div>皆辅养不得其道，而位势使之然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1183668_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下天资粹美，德性仁厚，必为有宋令主，但恨辅养之道有未至尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1183668_comment'></div>臣供职以来，六侍讲筵，但见诸臣拱手默坐，当讲者立案傍，解释数行而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1183668_comment'></div>如此，虽弥年积岁，所益几何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1183668_comment'></div>与周公辅养成王之道，殊不同矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1183668_comment'></div>或以为主上方幼，且当如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1183668_comment'></div>此不知本之论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1183668_comment'></div>古人生子，能食能言而教之小学之法，以豫为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1183668_comment'></div>人之幼也，知思未有所主，便当以格言至论日陈于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1183668_comment'></div>虽未晓知，且当薰聒，使盈耳充腹，久自安习，若固有之，虽以他言惑之，不能入也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1183668_comment'></div>若为之不豫，及乎稍长，私意偏好生于内，众口辩言铄于外，欲其纯完，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1183668_comment'></div>故所急在先入，岂有太早者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1183668_comment'></div>或又以为主上天资至美，自无违道，不须过虑，此尤非至论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1183668_comment'></div>夫圣莫圣于舜，而禹、皋陶未尝忘规戒，至曰「无若丹朱好慢游，作遨虐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1183668_comment'></div>且舜之不为慢游傲虐，虽至愚亦当知之，岂禹而不知乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1183668_comment'></div>盖处崇高之位，儆戒之道不得不如是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1183668_comment'></div>且人心岂有常哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1183668_comment'></div>以唐太宗之英睿，躬历艰难，力平祸乱，年亦长矣，始恶隋炀侈丽，毁其层观广殿，不六七年，复欲治乾阳殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1183668_comment'></div>是人心果可常乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1183668_comment'></div>所以圣贤虽明盛之际，不废规戒，为虑岂不深远也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1183668_comment'></div>况冲幼之君，闲邪拂违之道，可少懈乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1183668_comment'></div>伏自四月末閒，以暑热罢讲，比至中秋，盖踰三月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1183668_comment'></div>古人欲旦夕承弼，出入起居，而今乃三月不一见儒臣，何其与古人之意异也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1183668_comment'></div>今士大夫家子弟，亦不肯使经时累月不亲儒士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1183668_comment'></div>初秋渐凉，臣欲乞于内殿，或后苑清凉处，召见当日讲官，俾陈说道义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1183668_comment'></div>纵然未有深益，亦使天下知太皇太后用意如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1183668_comment'></div>又一人独对，与众见不同，自然情意易通，不三五次，便当习熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1183668_comment'></div>若不如此渐致，待其自然，是辅导官都不为力，将安用之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1183668_comment'></div>将来伏假既开，且乞依旧轮次直日，所贵常得一员独对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1183668_comment'></div>开发之道，盖自有方，朋习之益，最为至切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1183668_comment'></div>故周公辅成王，使伯禽与之处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1183668_comment'></div>圣人所为，必无不当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1183668_comment'></div>真庙使蔡伯希侍仁宗，乃师古也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1183668_comment'></div>臣欲乞择臣寮家子弟，十岁已上，十二已下，端谨颖悟者三人，侍上左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1183668_comment'></div>上所读之书，亦使读之，辨色则入，昏而罢归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1183668_comment'></div>常令二人入侍，一人更休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1183668_comment'></div>每人择有年宫人、内臣二人，随逐看承，不得暂离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1183668_comment'></div>常情笑语，亦勿禁止，唯须言语必正，举动必庄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1183668_comment'></div>仍使日至资善堂，呈所习业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1183668_comment'></div>讲官常加教劝，使知严惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1183668_comment'></div>年才十三，便令罢去，岁月之閒，自觉其益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1183668_comment'></div>自来宰臣十日一至经筵，亦止于默坐而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1183668_comment'></div>又间日讲读，则史官一人立侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1183668_comment'></div>史官之职，言动必书，施于视政时则可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1183668_comment'></div>经筵讲疑之所，乃燕处也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1183668_comment'></div>主上方问学之初，宜心泰体舒，乃能悦怿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1183668_comment'></div>今则前对大臣，动虞有失，旁立史官，言出辄书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1183668_comment'></div>使上欲游其志，得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1183668_comment'></div>欲发于言，敢乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1183668_comment'></div>深妨问学，不得不改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1183668_comment'></div>欲乞特降指挥，宰臣一月两次，与文彦博同赴经筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1183668_comment'></div>遇宰臣赴日，即乞就崇政殿讲说，因令史官入侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1183668_comment'></div>崇政殿说书之职，置来已久，乃是讲说之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1183668_comment'></div>汉、唐命儒士讲论，亦多在殿上，盖故事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1183668_comment'></div>迩英迫狭，讲读官、内臣近三十人在其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1183668_comment'></div>四月间尚未甚热，而讲官已流汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1183668_comment'></div>况主上气体嫩弱，岂得为便？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1183668_comment'></div>春夏之际，人气烝薄，深可虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1183668_comment'></div>祖宗之时，偶然在彼，执为典故，殊无义理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1183668_comment'></div>欲乞今后只于延和殿讲读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1183668_comment'></div>后楹垂帘，帘前置御座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1183668_comment'></div>太皇太后每遇政事稀简，圣体康和时，至帘下观讲官进说，不惟省察主上进业，于陛下圣聪，未必无补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1183668_comment'></div>兼讲官辅导之间，事意不少，有当奏禀，便得上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1183668_comment'></div>亦不可烦劳圣躬，限以日数，但旬月之间意适则往可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1183668_comment'></div>今讲读官共五人，四人皆兼要职，独臣不领别官，近复差修国子监太学条制，是亦兼他职也，乃无一人专职辅导者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1183668_comment'></div>执政之意可见也，盖惜人才，不欲使之闲尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1183668_comment'></div>又以为虽兼他职，不妨讲读，此尤不思之甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1183668_comment'></div>不敢言告君之道，只以告众人言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1183668_comment'></div>夫告于人者，非积其诚意，不能感而入也，故圣人以蒲卢喻政，谓以诚化之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1183668_comment'></div>今夫钟，怒而击之则武，悲而击之则哀，诚意之感而入也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1183668_comment'></div>告于人亦如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1183668_comment'></div>古人所以斋戒而告君者，何谓也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1183668_comment'></div>臣前后两得进讲，未尝敢不宿斋豫戒，潜思存诚，觊感动于上心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1183668_comment'></div>若使营营于职事，纷纷其思虑，待至上前，然后善其辞说，徒以颊舌感人，不亦浅乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1183668_comment'></div>此理，非知学者不能晓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1183668_comment'></div>道衰学废，世俗何尝闻此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1183668_comment'></div>虽闻之，必以为迂诞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1183668_comment'></div>陛下高识远见，当蒙鉴知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1183668_comment'></div>以朝廷之大，人主之重，置二三臣专职辅导，极非过当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1183668_comment'></div>今诸臣所兼皆要官，若未能遽罢，且乞免臣修国子监条制，俾臣夙夜精思竭诚，专在辅导。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1183668_comment'></div>不惟事理当然，且使天下知朝廷以为重事，不以为闲所也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1183668_comment'></div>陛下擢臣于草野之中，盖以其读圣人书，闻圣人道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1183668_comment'></div>臣敢不以其所学，上报圣明？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1183668_comment'></div>窃以圣人之学，不传久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1183668_comment'></div>臣幸得之于遗经，不自度量，以身任道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1183668_comment'></div>天下骇笑者虽多，而近年信从者亦众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1183668_comment'></div>方将区区驾其说以示学者，觊能传于后世，不虞天幸之至，得备讲说于人主之侧，使臣得以圣人之学，上沃圣聪，则圣人之道有可行之望，岂特臣之幸哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1183668_comment'></div>如陛下未以臣言为信，何不一赐访问？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1183668_comment'></div>臣当陈圣学之端绪，发至道之渊微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1183668_comment'></div>陛下圣鉴高明，必蒙照纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1183668_comment'></div>如其妄伪，愿从诛殛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1183668_comment'></div>臣愚不任恳悃惶惧待罪之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_140_1183668_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年8月</a>　差登闻鼓院，再辞不受。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　与司马光论学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年9月</a>　司马光卒，程颐主其丧事。作品：为太中祭司马温公文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　又上太皇太后疏。作品：上疏高太后。<div id='poem_1183657' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183657' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183657?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代富弼上神宗皇帝论永昭陵疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183657")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183657_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183657'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183657'>臣弼伏睹太皇太后山陵有期，老臣之心有所甚切，不忍不言，昧死以闻，惟陛下深思而力行之，不胜大愿！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183657_comment'></div>往者营奉昭陵时，英宗皇帝方不豫，未能听事，朝廷罔然不知其制，失于迫卒，不复深虑博访，凡百规画，一出匠者之拙谋，中人之私意，以巨木架石为之屋，计不百年，必当损坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183657_comment'></div>圹中又为铁罩，重且万斤，以木为骨，大止数寸，不过二三十年，决须摧毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183657_comment'></div>梓宫之厚度不盈尺，异日以亿万钧之石，自高而坠，其将奈何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183657_comment'></div>思之及此，骨寒胆丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183657_comment'></div>臣始则不知其详，后则无以为计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183657_comment'></div>士民之间有知之者，无不痛心饮恨，况老臣之心乎，况陛下之心乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183657_comment'></div>其后厚陵始为石藏，议者窃意主事大臣已悟昭陵之事，独陛下未知之尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183657_comment'></div>今也不幸，太皇太后奄弃天下之养，因此事会，当为之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183657_comment'></div>窃以周公制合葬之礼，仲尼善鲁人之祔，历代诸陵，虽不尽用，亦多行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183657_comment'></div>太祖皇帝神谋圣虑，超越万古，昭宪太后亦合安陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183657_comment'></div>夫以周公之制，仲尼之训，历代之旧，艺祖之法，循而行之，可无疑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183657_comment'></div>老臣愿陛下思安亲之道，为后日之虑，决于圣心，勿循浮议，奉太皇太后合祔昭陵，因得彻去铁罩，用厚陵石藏之制，仍更别加裁处，使异日虽木坏石坠，不能为害，救仁皇必至之祸，成陛下莫大之孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183657_comment'></div>复何难哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183657_comment'></div>在陛下断之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183657_comment'></div>既合礼典，又顺人情，虽无知之人必不敢以为非是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183657_comment'></div>但恐有以阴阳拘忌之说上惑圣聪者，在陛下睿断，不难辨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183657_comment'></div>不遵圣训，不度事宜，而规规于拘忌者，为贤乎，为愚乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183657_comment'></div>且阴阳之说，设为可信，吉凶之应，贵贱当同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183657_comment'></div>今天下臣庶之家，夫妇莫不同穴，未闻以为忌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1183657_comment'></div>独国家忌之，有何义理？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1183657_comment'></div>唐中宗庸昏之主，尚能守礼法，尽孝心，责严善思愚惑之论，卒祔乾陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1183657_comment'></div>其后高宗子孙历世延永，是合葬非不利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1183657_comment'></div>老臣位至三公，年将八十，复何求哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1183657_comment'></div>所保者名节而已，肯以不是事劝陛下取讥于后世乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1183657_comment'></div>复恐陛下谓臣心虽忠切，而识虑愚暗，不能晓达事理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1183657_comment'></div>臣诚至愚，然臣所言者，欲陛下守经典之训，遵艺祖之规，使仁宗皇帝得安全之道，于太皇太后极崇奉之意，岂独老臣之心哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1183657_comment'></div>天下之心莫不然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1183657_comment'></div>陛下不信，试以臣之所陈，访于群臣，必无以为非者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1183657_comment'></div>若以臣言为非，则是使仁宗遗骨圣体碎于巨石之下而不恤，乃为是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1183657_comment'></div>凡有血气之类，孰肯为此意乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1183657_comment'></div>臣事仁宗皇帝三十馀年，位至宰相，聋瞽之蔽，不能早知而救之于始，已为大罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1183657_comment'></div>今遇可为之时，若更惜情顾己，不能极言，天地神灵，必加诛殛死，何面目见仁宗于地下？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1183657_comment'></div>且陛下不知则已，今既闻之，在常人之情，无可忍而不为之理，况陛下至仁大孝乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1183657_comment'></div>惟陛下深思而力行之，则天下不胜大愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1183657_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1183657'>富公见托为此奏，颐以拙于文辞，辞之再三，其意甚切，义不可拒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1183657_comment'></div>数日之閒，遂生顾虑，不克上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1183657_comment'></div>惜乎其不果于义也，遂为忠孝罪人！</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1183657_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年1月25日</a>　罢讲一日。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年1月27日</a>　经筵毕，与宋哲宗皇帝交谈。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年2月15日</a>　讲“一言可终身行之”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年3月28日</a>　移讲延和殿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年4月6日</a>　依旧讲读迩英殿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　执政有欲用之为谏官者，程颐以书谢之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　在经筵每讲读必博引广喻，文彦博与吕范诸公交口称赞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　孔文仲弹劾程颐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　邵伯温入仕，程颐谆谆教诲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年6月12日</a>　刘绚卒，作祭文。作品：祭刘质夫。<div id='poem_1183788' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183788' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183788?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭刘质夫文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年6月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183788")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183788_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183788'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183788'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183788_comment'></div>圣学不传久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183788_comment'></div>吾生百世之后，志将明斯道、兴斯文于既绝，力小任重，而不惧其难者，盖亦有冀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183788_comment'></div>以谓茍能使知之者广，则用力者众，何难之不易也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183788_comment'></div>游吾门者众矣，而信之笃、得之多、行之果、守之固，若子者几希。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183788_comment'></div>方赖子致力以相辅，而不幸遽亡，使吾悲传学之难，则所以惜子者，岂止游从之情哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183788_comment'></div>兹焉归葬，不克临穴，姑因薄奠，以叙其哀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1183788_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年7月</a>　韩维罢相，离京师，程颐送别。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年8月2日</a>　罢经筵，差管勾西京国子监。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年11月6日</a>　乞归田里，不许。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年12月18日</a>　又乞归田里，不许。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　李籥卒，作祭文哀悼。作品：祭李端伯文。<div id='poem_1183789' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183789' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183789?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭李端伯文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183789")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183789_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183789'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183789'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183789_comment'></div>自予兄弟倡明道学，世方惊疑，能使学者视效而信从，子与刘质夫为有力矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183789_comment'></div>质夫于子为外兄弟，同邑而居，同门而学，才器相类，志尚如一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183789_comment'></div>予谓二子可以大受，期之远到，而半年之閒，相继以亡，使予忧事道者鲜，悲传学之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183789_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183789_comment'></div>天于斯文，何其艰哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183789_comment'></div>官制有拘，不克临穴，寄文为奠，以叙其哀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1183789_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年1月</a>　乞归田里，皆不报。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年2月</a>　乞致仕，又不报。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年2月</a>　三乞归田里，不报。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年</a>　代其父程珦作祭文悼念韩绛。作品：为太公祭韩康公文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年</a>　代人作书上宰相。作品：代人上宰相论郑白渠书。<div id='poem_1183713' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183713' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183713?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代人上宰相论郑白渠书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183713")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183713_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183713'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183713'>某闻天下之事，有甚难而易者，有甚易而难者，独系在上之人为与不为而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183713_comment'></div>昔韩欲罢秦兵，使郑国说以凿泾水溉田，注填阏之水，溉潟卤之地四万顷，亩收常一钟，关中遂为沃壤，无凶年，秦以富强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183713_comment'></div>至汉，白公复引泾水以溉田，民得其饶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183713_comment'></div>歌之曰：「田于何所？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183713_comment'></div>池阳谷口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183713_comment'></div>郑国在前，白渠起后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183713_comment'></div>衣食关中，亿万之口」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183713_comment'></div>此两渠之功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183713_comment'></div>秦、汉而下，皆获其利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183713_comment'></div>熙宁中，神宗皇帝讲求治功，兴葺遗利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183713_comment'></div>时先祖殿丞，建明郑、白之利，神宗皇帝赐对便殿，大称圣心，付以其事，兴役踰年，功已有叙，而害能者巧为沮止，不终厥功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183713_comment'></div>陕右之人，至今为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183713_comment'></div>某每思神宗皇帝知其利而欲兴之意，与先祖尽其力而被沮之恨，某未尝不愤叹至于流涕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183713_comment'></div>阁下尝尹长安矣，必闻其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183713_comment'></div>今则又非昔年之比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183713_comment'></div>泾水低下，渠口高仰，灌溉之功，几尽废矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183713_comment'></div>民用困乏，物斛踊贵，职此之由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183713_comment'></div>今方外有不顺之羌，师旅之兴，储备为急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183713_comment'></div>诚使秦中岁增谷数百千万斛，所济岂不甚大？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183713_comment'></div>某关西陋儒也，自幼小稔知其事，人微处远，无由自伸其愤郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1183713_comment'></div>幸遇仆射相公，以经纬之才，逢时得君，以天下事为己任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1183713_comment'></div>某是以不敢避狂妄之诛，尘渎钧听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1183713_comment'></div>倘蒙采录，或致成功，不使先祖抱恨泉下，则某平生志愿足矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1183713_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

广汉
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='86630aa1fc514f7b9634e980178810cb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("86630aa1fc514f7b9634e980178810cb");'><span id='86630aa1fc514f7b9634e980178810cb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1070')">1067-1070年</a>，35-38岁</div><div id='86630aa1fc514f7b9634e980178810cb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年</a>　随父至汉州。代其父程珦上神宗皇帝书论薄葬。作品：代其父上书论薄葬。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年</a>　为其父作《试汉州学生策问》三首。<div id='poem_1183764' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183764' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183764?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为家君作试汉州学策问三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>第一</a><span class='authorDate'>（1068年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183764")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183764_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183764'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183764'>问：士之所以贵乎人伦者，以明道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183764_comment'></div>若止于治声律、为禄利而已，则与夫工技之事，将何异乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183764_comment'></div>夫所谓道，固若大路然，人皆可勉而至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183764_comment'></div>如不可学而至，则古圣人何为教之勤勤如是，岂其欺后世邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183764_comment'></div>然学之之道当如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183764_comment'></div>后之儒者，莫不以为文章、治经术为务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183764_comment'></div>文章则华靡其词，新奇其意，取悦人耳目而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183764_comment'></div>经术则解释辞训，较先儒短长，立异说以为己工而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183764_comment'></div>如是之学，果可至于道乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183764_comment'></div>仲尼之门，独称颜子为好学，则曰「不迁怒，不贰过」也，与今之学，不其异乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183764_comment'></div>或曰：如是则在修身谨行而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183764_comment'></div>夫检于行者，设曰勉强之可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183764_comment'></div>通诸心者，姑谨修而可能乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183764_comment'></div>况无诸中不能强于外也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183764_comment'></div>此为儒之本，谅诸君之所素存也，幸明辨而详著于篇。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1183764_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1183765' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183765' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183765?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>第二</a><span class='authorDate'>（1068年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183765_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183765'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183765'>问：圣人之道，传诸经学者，必以经为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183765_comment'></div>然而诸经之奥，多所难明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183765_comment'></div>今取其大要，各举其一以言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183765_comment'></div>夫《易》卦之德，曰元亨利贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183765_comment'></div>或为四：曰元也，亨也，利也，贞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183765_comment'></div>或为二：曰大亨也，利于贞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183765_comment'></div>其词既同，义可异乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183765_comment'></div>所以异者何谓？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183765_comment'></div>《春秋》垂褒贬之法，所贬则明矣，所褒者何事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183765_comment'></div>《诗》之美刺，圣人取其止乎礼义者，以为法于后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183765_comment'></div>晋武公身为并夺，《无衣》美之，其教安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183765_comment'></div>《书》为王者轨范，不独著圣王之事以为法也，亦存其失以示戒尔，《五子之歌》是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183765_comment'></div>如盘庚之迁国，穆王之训刑，为是而可法邪，为非而可戒邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183765_comment'></div>《礼记》杂出于汉诸儒所传，谬乱多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183765_comment'></div>考之，完合于圣人者，其篇有几？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183765_comment'></div>夫古人之学贵专，不以泛滥为贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183765_comment'></div>诸君之于经，必各有所治，人言其所学可也，惟毋泛毋略。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1183765_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1183766' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183766' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183766?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>第三</a><span class='authorDate'>（1068年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183766_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183766'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183766'>问：儒者积学于己，以待用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183766_comment'></div>当世之务，固当讲明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183766_comment'></div>若夫朝廷之治，君相谟之，斯无间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183766_comment'></div>以一郡而言，守之职岂不以养人为本？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183766_comment'></div>然而民产不制，何术以济乎困穷？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183766_comment'></div>吏繇有数，何道以宽乎力役？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183766_comment'></div>比闾无法，教化何由而可行？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183766_comment'></div>衣食不足，风俗何缘而可厚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183766_comment'></div>自唐而上，世有循吏，著之史册，何今世独无其人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183766_comment'></div>岂古之治不可行于今邪，抑为之者不得其道邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183766_comment'></div>思欲仰希前哲之为，上副圣朝之寄，何所施设而能及斯？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183766_comment'></div>诸君从事于学，既勤且久，为政之方，固当明其体要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183766_comment'></div>至于民俗利病，皆耳目之所接也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183766_comment'></div>愿陈高论，得以矜式。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1183766_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　兄程颢为御史，推择人才，以张载、程颐为称首。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　在汉州，有答张载书。作品：答横渠书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　侯世与见程颐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年10月</a>　作手书拜谢傅耆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　作蜀守记。<div id='poem_1183768' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183768' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183768?labeling=true' target='_blank'>记蜀守</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183768")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183768_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183768'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183768'>成都人称近时镇蜀之善者，莫如田元钧、文潞公，语不善者，必曰蒋堂、程戡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183768_comment'></div>故谣言曰：「彦博亏<span class='inlineComment2'>（亏犹言不如也。）</span>田况，程戡胜蒋堂」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183768_comment'></div>言最善之中田更优，不善之中程犹差胜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183768_comment'></div>予尝访之士大夫，以至闾里间，察其善不善之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183768_comment'></div>所谓善者，得民心之悦，固有可善焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183768_comment'></div>所谓最不善者，乃可谓最善者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183768_comment'></div>至今人言及蒋公时事，必有不乐之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183768_comment'></div>问其所不乐者，众口所同，惟三事而已：减损遨乐，毁后土庙及诸淫祠，伐江渎庙木修府舍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183768_comment'></div>其尤失人心者，节遨乐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183768_comment'></div>前蒋者数十年为政<span class='inlineComment2'>（后阙）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1183768_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　在蜀与二使者游三峡不乘轿亦不留名。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　邵康节代书寄程颐诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈襄领国子监荐程颐。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
成都
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='38b69c342ac04f3f84b7544dba5bc18b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("38b69c342ac04f3f84b7544dba5bc18b");'><span id='38b69c342ac04f3f84b7544dba5bc18b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>，39岁</div><div id='38b69c342ac04f3f84b7544dba5bc18b' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>和成都府路长官范纯仁交流为政纲要。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>过成都，与韩宗道讨论减免差役之事。<br /></div>
