-----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ab33d47d010d4452baea2756843d3639_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ab33d47d010d4452baea2756843d3639");'><span id='ab33d47d010d4452baea2756843d3639_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1077')">1073-1077年</a>，41-45岁</div><div id='ab33d47d010d4452baea2756843d3639' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年</a>　居洛，与韩维交游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年</a>　同朱光庭访邵雍，论学问道。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年</a>　叔父程璠卒于河南。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年10月</a>　彗星见，代吕公著应诏疏。<div id='poem_1183656' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183656' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183656?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代吕公著应诏上神宗皇帝书<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁八年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183656")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183656_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183656'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183656'>伏睹今月十三日诏敕，以彗出东方，许中外臣僚直言朝廷阙失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183656_comment'></div>臣自言事得罪，久去朝廷，无所补报，退就闲冗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183656_comment'></div>尚敢区区以言自进者，诚见陛下寅畏天命，有恐惧脩省之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183656_comment'></div>草莱之人，尚思效其忠恳，况臣世荷国恩，久忝近侍，虽罪衅之馀，敢不竭其愚诚，以应明诏？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183656_comment'></div>臣伏观前史所载，彗之为变多矣，鲜有无其应者，盖上天之意，非徒然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183656_comment'></div>今陛下既有警畏之心，当思消弭之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183656_comment'></div>且以今日之变，孰从而来？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183656_comment'></div>《书》曰：「天视自我民视，天听自我民听」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183656_comment'></div>岂非政之所致欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183656_comment'></div>如曰非政之由，则经为诬矣，臣复何言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183656_comment'></div>诏之所求，亦为虚设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183656_comment'></div>若以为政之所致，则改以顺天，在陛下而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183656_comment'></div>晏子所谓「可祝而来，亦可禳而去」也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183656_comment'></div>《传》曰：「天之有彗，以除秽也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183656_comment'></div>又曰：「所以除旧布新」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183656_comment'></div>臣愿陛下祗若天戒，思当除者何事，而当新者何道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183656_comment'></div>如曰旧政既善，无所可除，则天为诬矣，臣复何言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183656_comment'></div>若以为当求自新，则在陛下思之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183656_comment'></div>自非大无道之世，何尝不遇灾而惧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183656_comment'></div>然而能自新者盖寡，大率蔽于所欲，惑于所任，明不足以自辨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1183656_comment'></div>视是而为非，以邪而为正，败亡至而不寤，天亦不能戒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1183656_comment'></div>岂其恶存而好亡，憎治而喜乱哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1183656_comment'></div>亦惑而不能辨尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1183656_comment'></div>臣以为辨之非艰，顾不得其道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1183656_comment'></div>诚能省己之存心，考己之任人，察己之为政，思己之自处，然后质之人言，何惑之不可辨哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1183656_comment'></div>能辨其惑，则知所以应天自新之道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1183656_comment'></div>臣请为陛下辨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1183656_comment'></div>所谓省己之存心者：人君因亿兆以为尊，其抚之治之之道，当尽其至诚恻怛之心，视之如伤，动敢不慎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1183656_comment'></div>兢兢然惟惧一政之不顺于天，一事之不合于理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1183656_comment'></div>如此，王者之公心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1183656_comment'></div>若乃恃所据之势，肆求欲之心，以严法令、举条纲为可喜，以富国家、强兵甲为自得，锐于作为，快于自任，贪惑至于如此，迷错岂能自知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1183656_comment'></div>若是者，以天下徇其私欲者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1183656_comment'></div>勤身劳力，适足以致负败，夙兴夜寐，适足以招后悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1183656_comment'></div>以是而致善治者，未之闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1183656_comment'></div>愿陛下内省于心，有近于是者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1183656_comment'></div>茍有之，则天之所戒也，当改而自新者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1183656_comment'></div>所谓考己之任人者：夫王者之取人，以天下之公而不以己，求其见正而不求其从欲，逆心者求诸道，巽志者察其非，尚孜孜焉惧或失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1183656_comment'></div>此王者任人之公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1183656_comment'></div>若乃喜同而恶异，偏信而害明，谓彼所言者吾之所大欲也，悦而望之，信而惑之，至于甚恶而不察，恣欺而不悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1183656_comment'></div>推是而往，鹿可以为马矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1183656_comment'></div>愿陛下考己之任人，有近于是者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1183656_comment'></div>茍有之，则天之所戒也，当改而自新者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1183656_comment'></div>方陛下思治之初，未有所偏主，好恶取舍一以公议，天下谓之贤，陛下从而贤之者众矣，进之于朝者有矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1183656_comment'></div>及乎既有为也，皆以不合而去之，更用后来之人，皆昔未尝以为贤者也，然后议论无违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1183656_comment'></div>始之所贤者皆愚，始之未尝贤者皆贤，此为天下之公乎，己意之私乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1183656_comment'></div>自论议无违之后，逆耳怫心之言亦罕闻矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1183656_comment'></div>夫以居至尊之位，负出世之资，而不闻怫逆之言，可惧之大者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1183656_comment'></div>知人之难，虽至明不能无失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1183656_comment'></div>然至于朝合则为不世之贤，暮隙则有无穷之罪，颠错亦已甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1183656_comment'></div>在任人之道当改亦明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1183656_comment'></div>所谓察己之为政者：为政之道，以顺民心为本，以厚民生为本，以安而不扰为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1183656_comment'></div>陛下以今日之事，方于即位之初，民心为欢悦乎，为愁怨乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1183656_comment'></div>民生为阜足乎，为穷蹙乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1183656_comment'></div>政事为安之乎，为扰之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1183656_comment'></div>亿兆之口非不能言也，顾恐察之不审尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1183656_comment'></div>茍有不察，则天之所戒也，当改而自新者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1183656_comment'></div>所谓思己之自处者：圣人谓「亡者保其存者也，乱者有其治者也」，陛下必不以斯言为妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1183656_comment'></div>自古以来，何尝有以危亡为忧而至危亡者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1183656_comment'></div>惟其自谓治安而危亡卒至者则多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1183656_comment'></div>不识陛下平日自处，以天下为如何，圣心所自知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1183656_comment'></div>茍有忧危恐惧之心，常虑所任者非其人，所由者非其道，唯恐不闻天下之言，如此则圣王保天下之心也，上帝其鉴之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1183656_comment'></div>或以为已安且治，所任者当矣，所为者至矣，天下之言不足恤矣，如此则天之所戒也，当改而自新者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1183656_comment'></div>所谓质之人言者，当有其方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1183656_comment'></div>欲询之于众人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1183656_comment'></div>众人之言可使同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1183656_comment'></div>欲访之下民乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1183656_comment'></div>下民之言亦可为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1183656_comment'></div>察之以一人之心，而蔽之以众人之智，其可胜乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1183656_comment'></div>是不足以辨惑，而足以固其蔽尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1183656_comment'></div>臣以为在外一二老臣，事先朝数十年，久当大任，天下共知其非欺妄人也，知其非覆败邦家者也，臣愿陛下礼而问之，宜可信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1183656_comment'></div>及天下所谓贤人君子，陛下闻之于有为之前，而不在今日利害之间者，亦可访也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1183656_comment'></div>以是数者参考之，则所当改者何事，所当新者何道，固可见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1183656_comment'></div>天下之人，一闻诏音，莫不鼓舞相庆，谓陛下必能上应天心，召迎和气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1183656_comment'></div>臣以为唯至诚可以动天，在陛下诚意而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1183656_comment'></div>昔在商王中宗之时有桑谷之祥，高宗之时有雊雉之异，二王以为惧而修政，遂致王道复兴，皆为商宗，百世之下颂其圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1183656_comment'></div>近世以来，引咎之诏，自新之言，亦常有之，倘人君不由于至诚，则天下徒以为虚语，其能感天心弭灾变乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1183656_comment'></div>臣愿陛下因此天戒，奋然改为，思商宗之休实，鉴后代之虚饰，不独消复灾沴于今日，将永保丕基于无穷，天下幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_76_1183656_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　张载弟张戬卒，评论张戬性情。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年7月</a>　范纯仁病笃，程颐往视之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>　张载再过洛见程颐，程颐赞“治体者，诚未有如子厚”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>　程颢论井田。<br ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年8月</a>　程珦葬弟程瑜、程璠于伊川，程颐主其事。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='8d98ead45ebb42fd915a4fb6ca95128a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8d98ead45ebb42fd915a4fb6ca95128a");'><span id='8d98ead45ebb42fd915a4fb6ca95128a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1084')">1082-1084年</a>，50-52岁</div><div id='8d98ead45ebb42fd915a4fb6ca95128a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年</a>　在洛，上文彦博求龙门庵第小简。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年</a>　在洛，答朱长文书。<div id='poem_1183703' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183703' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183703?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答朱长文书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1082年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183703")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183703_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183703'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183703'>相去之远，未知何日复为会合，人事固难前期也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183703_comment'></div>中前奉书，以足下心虚气损，奉劝勿多作诗文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183703_comment'></div>而见答之辞，乃曰：「为学上能探古先之陈迹，综群言之是非，欲其心通而默识之，固未能也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183703_comment'></div>又曰：「使后人见之，犹庶几曰不忘乎善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183703_comment'></div>茍不如是，诚惧没而无闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183703_comment'></div>此为学之末，宜兄之见责也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183703_comment'></div>使吾日闻夫子之道而忘乎此，岂不善哉<span class='inlineComment2'>（恐不记书中之言，故却录去。）</span>」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183703_comment'></div>此疑未得为至当之言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183703_comment'></div>某于朋友閒，其问不切者，未尝敢语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183703_comment'></div>以足下处疾，罕与人接，渴闻议论之益，故因此可论，而为吾弟尽其说，庶几有小补也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183703_comment'></div>向之云无多为文与诗者，非止为伤心气也，直以不当轻作尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183703_comment'></div>圣贤之言，不得已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183703_comment'></div>盖有是言，则是理明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183703_comment'></div>无是言，则天下之理有阙焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183703_comment'></div>如彼耒耜陶冶之器，一不制，则生人之道有不足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183703_comment'></div>圣人之言，虽欲已，得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183703_comment'></div>然其包涵尽天下之理，亦甚约也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183703_comment'></div>后之人，始执卷，则以文章为先，平生所为，动多于圣人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183703_comment'></div>然有之无所补，无之靡所阙，乃无用之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1183703", 1183703, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>赘言</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183703_comment'></div>不止赘而已，既不得其要，则离真失正，反害于道必矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1183703_comment'></div>诗之盛莫如唐，唐人善论文莫如韩愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1183703_comment'></div>愈之所称，独高李、杜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1183703_comment'></div>二子之诗，存者千篇，皆吾弟所见也，可考而知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1183703_comment'></div>茍足下所作皆合于道，足以辅翼圣人，为教于后，乃圣贤事业，何得为学之末乎，某何敢以此奉责？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1183703_comment'></div>又言欲使后人见其不忘乎善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1183703_comment'></div>人能为合道之文者，知道者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1183703_comment'></div>在知道者，所以为文之心，乃非区区惧其无闻于后，欲使后人见其不忘乎善而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1183703_comment'></div>此乃世人之私心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1183703_comment'></div>夫子「疾没世而名不称」焉者，疾没身无善可称云尔，非谓疾无名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1183703_comment'></div>名者可以厉中人，君子所存，非所汲汲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1183703_comment'></div>又云「上能探古先之陈迹，综群言之是非，欲其心通默识，固未能也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1183703_comment'></div>夫心通乎道，然后能辨是非，如持权衡以较轻重，孟子所谓知言是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1183703_comment'></div>揆之以道，则是非了然，不待精思而后见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1183703_comment'></div>学者当以道为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1183703_comment'></div>心不通乎道，而较古人之是非，犹不持权衡而酌轻重，竭其目力，劳其心智，虽使时中，亦古人所谓「亿则屡中」，君子不贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1183703_comment'></div>临纸遽书，不复思绎，故言无次序，多注改，勿讶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1183703_comment'></div>辞过烦矣，理或未安，却请示下，足以代面话。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1183703_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年</a>　认为作文害道。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年</a>　游嵩山，有诗。作品：游嵩山诗。<div id='poem_504871' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_504871' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/504871?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游嵩山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1082年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_504871")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_504871_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_504871'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_504871'>鞭羸百里远来游，岩谷<span class='inlineComment2'>（弘治本作数日）</span>阴云暝不收。<div id='poem_sentence_0_504871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_504871'>遮断好山教不见<span class='inlineComment2'>（弘治本作去）</span>，如何天意异人谋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_504871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_504871'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_504871_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年</a>　在洛，王佺期寄药，有诗酬谢。作品：寄谢王子真诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年</a>　兄程颢监汝州酒税，论汝州多瘿乃地气壅滞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年</a>　朱光庭、刘质夫过汝见程颐求学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年</a>　程珦与文彦博、司马康为同甲会。<br class='label1' id='1fbf926bd3724f0dadbeb2a92b963391_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1fbf926bd3724f0dadbeb2a92b963391");'><span id='1fbf926bd3724f0dadbeb2a92b963391_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年</a>，53岁</div><div id='1fbf926bd3724f0dadbeb2a92b963391' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年9月</a>　司马光、吕公著同荐程颐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年8月</a>　兄程颢卒，作明道行状。<div id='poem_1183778' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183778' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183778?labeling=true' target='_blank'>明道先生行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183778")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183778_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183778'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183778'>曾祖希振，任尚书虞部员外郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183778_comment'></div>妣，高密县君崔氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183778_comment'></div>祖遹，赠开府仪同三司、吏部尚书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183778_comment'></div>妣，孝感县太君张氏、长安县太君张氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183778_comment'></div>父珦，见任太中大夫，致仕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183778_comment'></div>母，寿安县君侯氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183778_comment'></div>先生名颢，字伯淳，姓程氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183778_comment'></div>其先曰乔伯，为周大司马，封于程，后遂以为氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183778_comment'></div>先生五世而上，居中山之博野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183778_comment'></div>高祖赠太子少师，讳羽，太宗朝以辅翊功显，赐第于京师，居再世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183778_comment'></div>曾祖而下，葬河南，今为河南人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183778_comment'></div>先生生而神气秀爽，异于常儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183778_comment'></div>未能言，叔祖母任氏太君抱之行，不觉钗坠，后数日方求之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183778_comment'></div>先生以手指示，随其所指而往，果得钗，人皆惊异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183778_comment'></div>数岁，诵诗书，强记过人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183778_comment'></div>十岁能为诗赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183778_comment'></div>十二三时，群居庠序中，如老成人，见者无不爱重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183778_comment'></div>故户部侍郎彭公思永谢客到学舍，一见异之，许妻以女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183778_comment'></div>踰冠，中进士第，调京兆府鄠县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183778_comment'></div>令以其年少，未知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1183778_comment'></div>民有借其兄宅以居者，发地中藏钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1183778_comment'></div>兄之子诉曰：「父所藏也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1183778_comment'></div>令曰：「此无證佐，何以决之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1183778_comment'></div>先生曰：「此易辨尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1183778_comment'></div>问兄之子曰：「尔父藏钱几何时矣」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1183778_comment'></div>曰：「四十年矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1183778_comment'></div>「彼借宅居几何时矣」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1183778_comment'></div>曰：「二十年矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1183778_comment'></div>即遣吏取钱十千视之，谓借宅者曰：「今官所铸钱，不五六年即遍天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1183778_comment'></div>此钱皆尔未居前数十年所铸，何也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1183778_comment'></div>其人遂服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1183778_comment'></div>令大奇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1183778_comment'></div>南山僧舍有石佛，岁传其首放光，远近男女聚观，昼夜杂处，为政者畏其神，莫敢禁止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1183778_comment'></div>先生始至，诘其僧曰：「吾闻石佛岁现光，有诸」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1183778_comment'></div>曰：「然」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1183778_comment'></div>戒曰：「俟复见，必先白吾，职事不能往，当取其首就观之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1183778_comment'></div>自是不复有光矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1183778_comment'></div>府境水害，仓卒兴役，诸邑率皆狼狈，惟先生所部，饮食茇舍无不安便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1183778_comment'></div>时盛暑，泄利大行，死亡甚众，独鄠人无死者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1183778_comment'></div>所至治役，人不劳而事集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1183778_comment'></div>尝谓人曰：「吾之董役，乃治军法也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1183778_comment'></div>当路者欲荐之，多问所欲，先生曰：「荐士当以才之所堪，不当问所欲」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1183778_comment'></div>再期，以避亲罢，再调江宁府上元县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1183778_comment'></div>田税不均，比他邑尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1183778_comment'></div>盖近府美田，为贵家富室以厚价薄其税而买之，小民茍一时之利，久则不胜其弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1183778_comment'></div>先生为令画法，民不知扰，而一邑大均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1183778_comment'></div>其始，富者不便，多为浮论，欲摇止其事，既而无一人敢不服者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1183778_comment'></div>后诸路行均税法，邑官不足，益以他官，经岁历时，文案山积，而尚有诉不均者，计其力比上元不啻千百矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1183778_comment'></div>会令罢去，先生摄邑事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1183778_comment'></div>上元剧邑，诉讼日不下二百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1183778_comment'></div>为政者疲于省览，奚暇及治道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1183778_comment'></div>先生处之有方，不阅月，民讼遂简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1183778_comment'></div>江南稻田，赖陂塘以溉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1183778_comment'></div>盛夏塘堤大决，计非千夫不可塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1183778_comment'></div>法当言之府，府禀于漕司，然后计功调役，非月馀不能兴作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1183778_comment'></div>先生曰：「比如是，苗槁久矣，民将何食？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1183778_comment'></div>救民获罪，所不辞也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1183778_comment'></div>遂发民塞之，岁则大熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1183778_comment'></div>江宁当水运之冲，舟卒病者则留之，为营以处，曰小营子，岁不下数百人，至者辄死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1183778_comment'></div>先生察其由，盖既留然后请于府给券，乃得食，比有司文具，则困于饥已数日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1183778_comment'></div>先生白漕司，给米贮营中，至者与之食，自是生全者大半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1183778_comment'></div>措置于纤微之间，而人已受赐，如此之比，所至多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1183778_comment'></div>先生常云：「一命之士，茍存心于爱物，于人必有所济」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1183778_comment'></div>仁宗登遐，遗制官吏成服，三日而除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1183778_comment'></div>三日之朝，府尹率群官将释服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1183778_comment'></div>先生进曰：「三日除服，遗诏所命，莫敢违也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1183778_comment'></div>请尽今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1183778_comment'></div>若朝而除之，所服止二日尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1183778_comment'></div>尹怒不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1183778_comment'></div>先生曰：「公自除之，某非至夜不敢释也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1183778_comment'></div>一府相视，无敢除者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1183778_comment'></div>茅山有龙池，其龙如蜴蜥而五色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1183778_comment'></div>祥符中，中使取二龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1183778_comment'></div>至中途，中使奏一龙飞空而去，自昔严奉以为神物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1183778_comment'></div>先生尝捕而脯之，使人不惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1183778_comment'></div>其始至邑，见人持竿道旁，以黏飞鸟，取其竿折之，教之使勿为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1183778_comment'></div>及罢官，舣舟郊外，有数人共语：「自主簿折黏竿，乡民子弟不敢畜禽鸟」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1183778_comment'></div>不严而令行，大率如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1183778_comment'></div>再期，就移泽州晋城令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1183778_comment'></div>泽人淳厚，尤服先生教命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1183778_comment'></div>民以事至邑者，必告之以孝弟忠信，入所以事父兄，出所以事长上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1183778_comment'></div>度乡村远近为伍保，使之力役相助、患难相恤，而奸伪无所容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1183778_comment'></div>凡孤茕残废者，责之亲戚乡党，使无失所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1183778_comment'></div>行旅出于其涂者，疾病皆有所养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1183778_comment'></div>诸乡皆有校，暇时亲至，召父老而与之语，儿童所读书，亲为正句读，教者不善，则为易置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1183778_comment'></div>俗始甚野，不知为学，先生择子弟之秀者，聚而教之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1183778_comment'></div>去邑才十馀年，而服儒服者盖数百人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1183778_comment'></div>乡民为社会，为立科条，旌别善恶，使有劝有耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1183778_comment'></div>邑几万室，三年之间，无强盗及斗死者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1183778_comment'></div>秩满，代者且至，吏夜叩门，称有杀人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1183778_comment'></div>先生曰：「吾邑安有此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1183778_comment'></div>诚有之，必某村某人也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1183778_comment'></div>问之果然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1183778_comment'></div>家人惊异，问何以知之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1183778_comment'></div>曰：「吾常疑此人恶少之弗革者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1183778_comment'></div>河东财赋窘迫，官所科买，岁为民患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1183778_comment'></div>虽至贱之物，至官取之，则其价翔踊，多者至数十倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1183778_comment'></div>先生常度所需，使富家预储，定其价而出之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1183778_comment'></div>富室不失倍息，而乡民所费，比常岁十不过二三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1183778_comment'></div>民税常移近边，载往则道远，就籴则价高，先生择富民之可任者，预使购粟边郡，所费大省，民力用纾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1183778_comment'></div>县库有杂纳钱数百千，常借以补助民力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1183778_comment'></div>部使者至，则告之曰：「此钱令自用而不敢私，请一切不问」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1183778_comment'></div>使者屡更，无不从者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1183778_comment'></div>先时民惮差役，役及则互相纠诉，乡邻遂为仇雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1183778_comment'></div>先生尽知民产厚薄，第其先后，按籍而命之，无有辞者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1183778_comment'></div>河东义勇，农隙则教以武事，然应文备数而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1183778_comment'></div>先生至，晋城之民遂为精兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1183778_comment'></div>晋俗尚焚尸，虽孝子慈孙，习以为安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1183778_comment'></div>先生教谕禁止，民始信之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1183778_comment'></div>而先生去后，郡官有母死者，惮于远致，以投烈火，愚俗视效，先生之教遂废，识者恨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1183778_comment'></div>先生为令，视民如子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1183778_comment'></div>欲辨事者，或不持牒，径至庭下，陈其所以，先生从容告语，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_111_1183778", 1183778, "Clauses/336/Comments/0")'>谆谆不倦</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1183778_comment'></div>在邑三年，百姓爱之如父母，去之日，哭声振野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1183778_comment'></div>用荐者，改著作佐郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1183778_comment'></div>寻以御史中丞吕公公著荐，授太子中允，权监察御史里行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1183778_comment'></div>神宗素知先生名，召对之日，从容咨访，比二三见，遂期以大用，每将退，必曰：「频求对来，欲常相见尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1183778_comment'></div>一日，论议甚久，日官报午正，先生遽求退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1183778_comment'></div>庭中中人相谓曰：「御史不知上未食邪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1183778_comment'></div>前后进说甚多，大要以正心窒欲，求贤育材为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1183778_comment'></div>先生不饰辞辨，独以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_119_1183778", 1183778, "Clauses/365/Comments/0")'>诚意</span>感动人主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1183778_comment'></div>神宗尝使推择人才，先生所荐者数十人，而以父表弟张载暨弟颐为首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1183778_comment'></div>所上章疏，子侄不得窥其稿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1183778_comment'></div>尝言：「人主当防未萌之欲」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1183778_comment'></div>神宗俯身拱手曰：「当为卿戒之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1183778_comment'></div>及因论人才，曰：「陛下奈何轻天下士」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1183778_comment'></div>神宗曰：「朕何敢如是」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1183778_comment'></div>言之至于再三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1183778_comment'></div>时王荆公安石日益信用，先生每进见，必为神宗陈君道以至诚仁爱为本，未尝及功利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1183778_comment'></div>神宗始疑其迂，而礼貌不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1183778_comment'></div>尝极陈治道，神宗曰：「此尧、舜之事，朕何敢当」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1183778_comment'></div>先生愀然曰：「陛下此言，非天下之福也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1183778_comment'></div>荆公浸行其说，先生意多不合，事出必论列，数月之间，章数十上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1183778_comment'></div>尤极论者：辅臣不同心，小臣与大计，公论不行，青苗取息，卖祠部牒，差提举官多非其人及不经封駮，京东转运司剥民希宠不加黜责，兴利之臣日进，尚德之风浸衰等十馀事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1183778_comment'></div>荆公与先生虽道不同，而尝谓先生忠信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1183778_comment'></div>先生每与论事，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_134_1183778", 1183778, "Clauses/412/Comments/0")'>心平气和</span>，荆公多为之动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1183778_comment'></div>而言路好直者，必欲力攻取胜，由是与言者为敌矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1183778_comment'></div>先生言既不行，恳求外补，神宗犹重其去，上章及面请至十数，不许，遂阖门待罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1183778_comment'></div>神宗将黜诸言者，命执政除先生监司，差权发遣京西路提点刑狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1183778_comment'></div>复上章曰：「臣言是愿行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1183778_comment'></div>如其妄言，当赐显责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1183778_comment'></div>请罪而获迁，刑赏混矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1183778_comment'></div>累请得罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1183778_comment'></div>既而神宗手批，暴白同列之罪，独于先生无责，改差签书镇宁军节度判官事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1183778_comment'></div>为守者严刻多忌，通判而下，莫敢与辩事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1183778_comment'></div>始意先生尝任台宪，必不尽力职事，而又虑其慢己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1183778_comment'></div>既而先生事之甚恭，虽筦库细务，无不尽心，事小未安，必与之辨，遂无不从者，相与甚欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1183778_comment'></div>屡平反重狱，得不死者前后盖十数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1183778_comment'></div>河清卒于法不他役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1183778_comment'></div>时中人程昉为外都水丞，怙势，蔑视州郡，欲尽取诸埽兵治二股河，先生以法拒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1183778_comment'></div>昉请于朝，命以八百人与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1183778_comment'></div>天方大寒，昉肆其虐，众逃而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1183778_comment'></div>州官晨集城门，吏报河清兵溃归，将入城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1183778_comment'></div>众官相视，畏昉欲弗纳，先生曰：「此逃死自归，弗纳必为乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1183778_comment'></div>昉有言，某自当之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1183778_comment'></div>即亲往，开门抚谕，约归休三日复役，众欢呼而入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1183778_comment'></div>具以事上闻，得不复遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1183778_comment'></div>后昉奏事过州，见先生，言甘而气慑，既而扬言于众曰：「澶卒之溃，乃程中允诱之，吾必诉于上」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1183778_comment'></div>同列以告，先生笑曰：「彼方惮我，何能尔也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1183778_comment'></div>果不敢言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1183778_comment'></div>会曹村埽决，时先生方救护小吴，相去百里，州帅刘公涣以事急告，先生一夜驰至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1183778_comment'></div>帅俟于河桥，先生谓帅曰：「曹村决，京城可虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1183778_comment'></div>臣子之分，身可塞亦为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1183778_comment'></div>请尽以厢兵见付，事或不集，公当亲率禁兵以继之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1183778_comment'></div>帅义烈士，遂以本镇印授先生，曰：「君自用之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1183778_comment'></div>先生得印，不暇入城省亲，径走决堤，谕士卒曰：「朝廷养尔辈，正为缓急尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1183778_comment'></div>尔知曹村决则注京城乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1183778_comment'></div>吾与尔曹以身捍之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1183778_comment'></div>众皆感激自效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1183778_comment'></div>论者皆以为势不可塞，徒劳人尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1183778_comment'></div>先生命善泅者衔细绳以渡，决口水方奔注，达者百一，卒能引大索以济众，两岸并进，昼夜不息，数日而合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1183778_comment'></div>其将合也，有大木自中流而下，先生顾谓众曰：「得彼巨木横流入口，则吾事济矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1183778_comment'></div>语才已，木遂横，众以为至诚所致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1183778_comment'></div>其后曹村之下复决，遂久不塞，数路困扰，大为朝廷忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1183778_comment'></div>人以为，使先生在职，安有是也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1183778_comment'></div>郊祀霈恩，先生曰：「吾罪涤矣，可以去矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1183778_comment'></div>遂求监局，以便亲养，得罢归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1183778_comment'></div>自是丑正者竞扬避新法之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1183778_comment'></div>岁馀，得监西京洛河竹木务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1183778_comment'></div>荐者言其未尝叙年劳，丐迁秩，特改太常丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1183778_comment'></div>神宗犹念先生，会修三经义，尝语执政曰：「程某可用」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1183778_comment'></div>执政不对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1183778_comment'></div>又尝有登对者自洛至，问曰：「程某在彼否」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1183778_comment'></div>连言佳士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1183778_comment'></div>其后彗见翼轸间，诏求直言，先生应诏论朝政极切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1183778_comment'></div>还朝，执政屡进拟，神宗皆不许，既而手批与府界知县，差知扶沟县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1183778_comment'></div>先生诣执政，复求监当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1183778_comment'></div>执政谕以上意不可改也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1183778_comment'></div>数月，右府同荐，除判武学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1183778_comment'></div>新进者言其新法之初，首为异论，罢复旧任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1183778_comment'></div>先生为治，专尚宽厚，以教化为先，虽若甚迂，而民实风动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1183778_comment'></div>扶沟素多盗，虽乐岁，强盗不减十馀发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1183778_comment'></div>先生在官，无强盗者几一年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1183778_comment'></div>广济蔡河出县境，濒河不逞之民，不复治生业，专以胁取舟人物为事，岁必焚舟十数以立威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1183778_comment'></div>先生始至，捕得一人，使引其类，得数十人，不复根治旧恶，分地而处之，使以挽舟为业，且察为恶者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1183778_comment'></div>自是邑境无焚舟之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1183778_comment'></div>畿邑田税重，朝廷岁常蠲除以为惠泽，然而良善之民惮督责而先输，逋负获除者皆顽民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1183778_comment'></div>先生为约，前料获免者，今必如期而足，于是惠泽始均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1183778_comment'></div>司农建言，天下输役钱，达户四等，而畿内独止第三，请亦及第四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1183778_comment'></div>先生力陈不可，司农奏其议，谓必获罪，而神宗是之，畿邑皆得免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1183778_comment'></div>先生为政，常权谷价，不使至甚贵甚贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1183778_comment'></div>会大旱，麦苗且枯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1183778_comment'></div>先生教人掘井以溉，一井不过数工，而所灌数亩，阖境赖焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1183778_comment'></div>水灾民饥，先生请发粟贷之，邻邑亦请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1183778_comment'></div>司农怒，遣使阅实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1183778_comment'></div>使至邻邑，而令遽自陈谷且登，无贷可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1183778_comment'></div>使至，谓先生盍亦自陈？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1183778_comment'></div>先生不肯，使者遂言不当贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1183778_comment'></div>先生力言民饥，请贷不已，道得谷六千石，饥者用济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1183778_comment'></div>而司农益怒，视贷籍户同等而所贷不等，檄县杖主吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1183778_comment'></div>先生言，济饥当以口之众寡，不当以户之高下，且令实为之，非吏罪，乃得已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1183778_comment'></div>内侍都知王中正巡阅保甲，权宠至盛，所至淩慢县官，诸邑供帐，竞务华鲜，以悦奉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1183778_comment'></div>主吏以请，先生曰：「吾邑贫，安能效他邑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1183778_comment'></div>且取于民，法所禁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1183778_comment'></div>今有故青帐，可用之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1183778_comment'></div>先生在邑岁馀，中正往来境上，卒不入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1183778_comment'></div>邻邑有冤诉府，愿得先生决之者，前后五六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1183778_comment'></div>有犯小盗者，先生谓曰：「汝能改行，吾薄汝罪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1183778_comment'></div>盗叩首愿自新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1183778_comment'></div>后数月，复穿窬，捕吏及门，盗告其妻曰：「我与大丞约，不复为盗，今何面目见之邪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1183778_comment'></div>遂自经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1183778_comment'></div>官制改，除奉议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1183778_comment'></div>朝廷遣官括牧地，民田当没者千顷，往往持累世契券以自明，皆弗用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1183778_comment'></div>诸邑已定，而扶沟民独不服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1183778_comment'></div>遂有朝旨，改税作租，不复加益，及听卖易如私田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1183778_comment'></div>民既倦于追呼，又得不加赋，乃皆服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1183778_comment'></div>先生以为不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1183778_comment'></div>括地官至，谓先生曰：「民愿服而君不许，何也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1183778_comment'></div>先生曰：「民徒知今日不加赋，而不知后日增租夺田，则失业无以生矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1183778_comment'></div>因为言仁厚之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1183778_comment'></div>其人感动，谢曰：「宁受责，不敢违公」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1183778_comment'></div>遂去之他邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1183778_comment'></div>不踰月，先生罢去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1183778_comment'></div>其人复至，谓摄令者曰：「程奉议去矣，尔复何恃而敢稽违朝旨」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1183778_comment'></div>督责甚急，数日而事集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1183778_comment'></div>邻邑民犯盗，系县狱而逸，既又遇赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1183778_comment'></div>先生坐是以特旨罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1183778_comment'></div>邑人知先生且罢，诣府及司农丐留者千数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1183778_comment'></div>去之日，不使人知，老稚数百，追及境上，攀挽号泣，遣之不去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1183778_comment'></div>以亲老求近乡监局，得监汝州酒税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1183778_comment'></div>今上嗣位，覃恩，改承议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1183778_comment'></div>先生虽小官，贤士大夫视其进退，以卜兴衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1183778_comment'></div>圣政方新，贤德登进，先生特为时望所属，召为宗正寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1183778_comment'></div>未行，以疾终，元丰八年六月十五日也，享年五十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1183778_comment'></div>士大夫识与不识，莫不哀伤，为朝廷生民恨惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1183778_comment'></div>先生资禀既异，而充养有道，纯粹如精金，温润如良玉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1183778_comment'></div>宽而有制，和而不流；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1183778_comment'></div>忠诚贯于金石，孝弟通于神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1183778_comment'></div>视其色，其接物也如春阳之温；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1183778_comment'></div>听其言，其入人也如时雨之润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1183778_comment'></div>胸怀洞然，彻视无间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1183778_comment'></div>测其蕴，则浩乎若沧溟之无际；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1183778_comment'></div>极其德，美言盖不足以形容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1183778_comment'></div>先生行己，内主于敬，而行之以恕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1183778_comment'></div>见善若出于己，不欲勿施于人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1183778_comment'></div>居广居而行大道，言有物而动有常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1183778_comment'></div>先生为学，自十五六时，闻汝南周茂叔论道，遂厌科举之业，慨然有求道之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1183778_comment'></div>未知其要，泛滥于诸家，出入于老、释者几十年，返求诸《六经》而后得之，明于庶物，察于人伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1183778_comment'></div>知尽性至命，必本于孝悌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1183778_comment'></div>穷神知化，由通于礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1183778_comment'></div>辨异端似是之非，开百代未明之惑，秦、汉而下，未有臻斯理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1183778_comment'></div>谓孟子没而圣学不传，以兴起斯文为己任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1183778_comment'></div>其言曰：「道之不明，异端害之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1183778_comment'></div>昔之害近而易知，今之害深而难辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1183778_comment'></div>昔之惑人也，乘其迷暗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1183778_comment'></div>今之入人也，因其高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1183778_comment'></div>自谓之穷神知化，而不足以开物成务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1183778_comment'></div>言为无不周遍，实则外于伦理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1183778_comment'></div>穷深极微，而不可以入尧、舜之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1183778_comment'></div>天下之学，非浅陋固滞，则必入于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1183778_comment'></div>自道之不明也，邪诞妖异之说竞起，涂生民之耳目，溺天下于污浊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1183778_comment'></div>虽高才明智，胶于见闻，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_270_1183778", 1183778, "Clauses/829/Comments/0")'>醉生梦死</span>，不自觉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1183778_comment'></div>是皆正路之蓁芜，圣门之蔽塞，辟之而后可以入道」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1183778_comment'></div>先生进将觉斯人，退将明之书，不幸早世，皆未及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1183778_comment'></div>其辨析精微，稍见于世者，学者之所传尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1183778_comment'></div>先生之门，学者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1183778_comment'></div>先生之言，平易易知，贤愚皆获其益，如群饮于河，各充其量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1183778_comment'></div>先生教人，自致知至于知止，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_276_1183778", 1183778, "Clauses/850/Comments/0")'>诚意</span>至于平天下，洒扫应对至于穷理尽性，循循有序；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1183778_comment'></div>病世之学者舍近而趋远，处下而窥高，所以轻自大而卒无得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1183778_comment'></div>先生接物，辨而不閒，感而能通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1183778_comment'></div>教人而人易从，怒人而人不怨，贤愚善恶咸得其心，狡伪者献其诚，暴慢者致其恭，闻风者诚服，觌德者心醉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1183778_comment'></div>虽小人以趋向之异，顾于利害，时见排斥，退而省其私，未有不以先生为君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1183778_comment'></div>先生为政，治恶以宽，处烦而裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1183778_comment'></div>当法令繁密之际，未尝从众，为应文逃责之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1183778_comment'></div>人皆病于拘碍，而先生<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_283_1183778", 1183778, "Clauses/878/Comments/0")'>处之绰然</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1183778_comment'></div>众忧以为甚难，而先生为之沛然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1183778_comment'></div>虽当仓卒，不动声色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_285_1183778_comment'></div>方监司竞为严急之时，其待先生，率皆宽厚，设施之际，有所赖焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_286_1183778_comment'></div>先生所为纲条法度，人可效而为也，至其道之而从，动之而和，不求物而物应，未施信而民信，则人不可及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_287_1183778_comment'></div>彭夫人封仁和县君，严正有礼，事舅以孝称，善睦其族，先一年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_288_1183778_comment'></div>子曰端懿，蔡州汝阳县主簿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_289_1183778_comment'></div>曰端本，治进士业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1183778_comment'></div>女适假承务郎朱纯之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1183778_comment'></div>卜以今年十月乙酉，葬于伊川先茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1183778_comment'></div>谨书家世行业及历官行事之大概，以求志于作者，谨状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1183778_comment'></div>元丰八年八月日弟颐状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_294_1183778_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年9月</a>　求韩维、孙永求为兄程颢作墓志。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年</a>　答杨时书。作品：答杨时慰书。<div id='poem_1183707' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183707' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183707?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答杨时慰书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183707")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183707_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183707'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183707'>颐泣启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183707_comment'></div>颐罪恶不弟，感招祸变，不自死灭，兄长丧亡，哀苦怨痛，肝心摧裂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183707_comment'></div>日月迅速，忽将三月，追思痛切，不可堪处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183707_comment'></div>远承慰问，及寄示祭文哀辞，足见岁寒之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183707_comment'></div>家兄道学行义，足以泽世垂后，不幸至此，天乎奈何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183707_comment'></div>颐悲苦之馀，仅存气息，筋骸支离，尤倦执笔，况哀诚非书所能尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183707_comment'></div>所幸老父经此烦恼，饮食起居如常，不烦深虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183707_comment'></div>伏纸摧咽，言不伦次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183707_comment'></div>颐泣启杨君法曹<span class='inlineComment2'>（九月十二日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183707_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1183707'>十月二十四日葬，韩持国为志，行状颐自作，徐当寄去。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1183707_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年10月24日</a>　韩维卒，作行状。作品：韩维行状。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年10月24日</a>　葬兄程颢于伊川先茔，同日葬孝女于伊川先茔之东。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年10月</a>　葬兄程颢于伊川先茔，为墓表作序。作品：明道先生墓表序。<div id='poem_1183781' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183781' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183781?labeling=true' target='_blank'>明道先生墓表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183781")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183781_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183781'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183781'>先生名颢，字伯淳，葬于伊川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183781_comment'></div>潞国太师题其墓曰「明道先生」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183781_comment'></div>弟颐序其所以而刻之石曰：周公没，圣人之道不行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183781_comment'></div>孟轲死，圣人之学不传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183781_comment'></div>道不行，百世无善治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183781_comment'></div>学不传，千载无真儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183781_comment'></div>无善治，士犹得以明夫善治之道，以淑诸人，以传诸后；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183781_comment'></div>无真儒，天下贸贸焉莫知所之，人欲肆而天理灭矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183781_comment'></div>先生生千四百年之后，得不传之学于遗经，志将以斯道觉斯民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183781_comment'></div>天不憖遗，哲人早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183781_comment'></div>乡人士大夫相与议曰：道之不明也久矣，先生出，倡圣学以示人，辨异端，辟邪说，开历古之沉迷，圣人之道得先生而后明，为功大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183781_comment'></div>于是帝师采众议而为之称以表其墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183781_comment'></div>学者之于道，知所向，然后见斯人之为功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183781_comment'></div>知所至，然后见斯名之称情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183781_comment'></div>山可夷，谷可湮，明道之名亘万世而长存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183781_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1183781", 1183781, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>勒石</span>墓傍，以诏后人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183781_comment'></div>元丰乙丑十月戊子书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1183781_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年</a>　谢良佐侍行问佛儒之别。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年</a>　朱光庭过洛见程颐。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='69ed190f4a114e0386352b0c292740ea_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("69ed190f4a114e0386352b0c292740ea");'><span id='69ed190f4a114e0386352b0c292740ea_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1090')">1089-1090年</a>，57-58岁</div><div id='69ed190f4a114e0386352b0c292740ea' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年</a>　判西京国子监，文彦博为西京长官，尊礼之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年</a>　在洛阳，与范祖禹有书信往来。作品：寄范公淳夫书。<div id='poem_1183733' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183733' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183733?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄范淳夫书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1089年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183733")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183733_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183733'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183733'>丞相久留，左右所助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183733_comment'></div>一意正道者，实在原明耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183733_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1183733_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年2月</a>　在洛阳，代其父程珦祭吕公著。作品：为太中祭吕申公文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年11月</a>　代其父程珦为家藏太宗墨宝作跋文。作品：为太中书家藏太宗宝字后。<div id='poem_1183740' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183740' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183740?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为家君书家藏太宗皇帝宝字后</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐四年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183740")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183740_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183740'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183740'>先臣少师，以府僚事太宗皇帝于开封，被眷特异，前后所赐亲笔多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183740_comment'></div>天圣中，遭家难，诸父继亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183740_comment'></div>臣时未冠，复在远方，京师赐第，外姻守之，宝藏之物，既于盗手，于今在者，乃其遗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183740_comment'></div>故太宗亲书惟存十三字，其六乃开封文移，皆缘祭祀及贡举事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183740_comment'></div>臣恭思太宗皇帝以介弟之贵，晋王之重，尹正天府，而常事之小者，皆亲书之<span class='inlineComment2'>（自来大臣领州小事，多不亲书。）</span>，圣心可见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183740_comment'></div>盖于祀事之严，取士之重，虽细故必亲，诚孝恭虔之心也，急贤好士之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183740_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183740_comment'></div>成万世无穷之基，岂不由是心乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183740_comment'></div>愚臣窃谓，是心也宜为后圣法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183740_comment'></div>元祐四年己巳十一月癸未，太中大夫致仕、上柱国、永年县开国伯、食邑九百户臣程珦谨题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1183740_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年1月13日</a>　父程珦以疾终于西京国子监公舍。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年4月15日</a>　葬其父程珦伊川先茔。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年</a>　葬其父程珦伊川先茔，作家传。作品：太中家传。上谷郡君家书。<div id='poem_1183779' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183779' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183779?labeling=true' target='_blank'>先公太中家传</a><span class='authorDate'>（1090年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183779")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183779_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183779'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183779'>先公太中讳珦，字伯温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183779_comment'></div>旧名温，字君玉，既登朝，改后名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183779_comment'></div>景德三年丙午正月二十三日，生于京师泰宁坊赐第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183779_comment'></div>性仁孝温厚，恪勤畏慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183779_comment'></div>开府事父兄谨敬过人，责子弟甚严，公才十馀岁，则使治家事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183779_comment'></div>事有小不称意旨，公恐惧若无所容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183779_comment'></div>自少为族兄文简公所器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183779_comment'></div>开府终于黄陂，公年始冠，诸父继亡，聚属甚众，无田园可依，遂寓居黄陂，劳身苦志，奉养诸母，教抚弟妹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183779_comment'></div>时长弟璠七岁，从弟瑜六岁，馀皆孩幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183779_comment'></div>后数岁，朝廷录旧臣之后，授公郊社斋郎，以口众不能偕行，遂不赴调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183779_comment'></div>文简公义之，为请于朝，就注黄陂县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183779_comment'></div>任满，又不能调，闲居安贫，以待诸弟之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183779_comment'></div>至长弟与从弟皆得官娶妇，二妹既嫁，乃复赴调，授吉州庐陵县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183779_comment'></div>时刘丞相沆已贵显，其子弟有恃势暴横于乡里者，郡守以下皆为之屈，公独不与接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183779_comment'></div>刘丞相闻而愧之，待公甚厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183779_comment'></div>再调润州观察支使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183779_comment'></div>有侍禁曹元哲者，挟权要势，与人争田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183779_comment'></div>守畏逼，属公右之，公弗为挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183779_comment'></div>润当途，事烦剧，多赖公以济，声闻甚著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183779_comment'></div>部使者至，无有不论荐者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1183779_comment'></div>改大理寺丞，知虔州兴国县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1183779_comment'></div>虔人素号难治，而邑之衣锦乡尤为称首，自昔治之与他乡异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1183779_comment'></div>前令欲以惨酷威之，盛冬使争者对立于庭，以雪埋及膝，而人益不服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1183779_comment'></div>公善告谕之，与他乡一视，人遂信服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1183779_comment'></div>在邑几二年，而狱空者岁馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1183779_comment'></div>江西狡民善为古券契，田讼最为难辨，而虔尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1183779_comment'></div>旁邑有争，积十馀岁不能决，部使者以委公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1183779_comment'></div>根连證佐，嚣然盈庭，公独呼争者前讯之，不十数语，尽得其情，遂皆服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1183779_comment'></div>事决于顷刻之閒，人以为神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1183779_comment'></div>就移知龚州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1183779_comment'></div>时宜州反獠欧希范既诛，乡人忽传其降，言当为我南海立祠，于是迎其神以往，自宜至龚，历数州矣，莫之禁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1183779_comment'></div>公使诘之，对曰：「过浔州，守以为妖，投奉神之具于江中，逆流而上，守惧，乃更致礼」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1183779_comment'></div>公曰：「试再投之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1183779_comment'></div>越人畏鬼，甚于畏官，皆莫敢前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1183779_comment'></div>公杖不奉命者，及投之，乃流去，人方信其为妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1183779_comment'></div>在州二岁，部使者未尝入境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1183779_comment'></div>时潘师旦为提点刑狱，最称严察，一道𢥠畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1183779_comment'></div>尝过境上，以书谢公曰：「既闻清治，不须至也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1183779_comment'></div>迁太子中舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1183779_comment'></div>明堂覃恩，改殿中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1183779_comment'></div>代还在涂，而侬智高作乱，破州城，后守贷死羁置，人皆以公获免为积善之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1183779_comment'></div>授知徐州沛县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1183779_comment'></div>会久雨，平原出水，谷既不登，晚种不入，民无卒岁具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1183779_comment'></div>公谓俟可耕而种，则时已过矣，乃募富家，得豆数千石以贷民，使布之水中，水未尽涸而甲已露矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1183779_comment'></div>是年，遂不艰食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1183779_comment'></div>有丐于市者，自称僧伽之弟，愚者相倡，争遗金钱，公杖之而出诸境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1183779_comment'></div>迁国子博士，赐绯鱼袋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1183779_comment'></div>归监在京西染院，迁尚书虞部员外郎，知凤州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1183779_comment'></div>凤当川、蜀之冲，轺传旁午，毁誉易得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1183779_comment'></div>为守者相承，务丰厨传，主吏多至破产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1183779_comment'></div>公裁减几半，曰：「是足以为礼，未为薄也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1183779_comment'></div>会汉中不稔，饥民自褒斜山谷而出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1183779_comment'></div>公教于路口为糜粥以待之，所济甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1183779_comment'></div>迁司门员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1183779_comment'></div>丁崇国太夫人忧，服除，权判鸿胪寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1183779_comment'></div>英宗嗣位，覃恩，迁库部员外郎，知磁州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1183779_comment'></div>磁城，赵简子所筑，东南隅水泉恶，灌濯亦不可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1183779_comment'></div>居民安于久习，妇女晨出远汲，不惟劳，且乏用，风俗以之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1183779_comment'></div>历千馀岁，无为虑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1183779_comment'></div>公度城曲之地，曰：「此去濠水数步之近，渐渍既久，地脉当变矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1183779_comment'></div>穿二井，果美泉也，人甚赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1183779_comment'></div>时久雨，自河以北，城垒皆圮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1183779_comment'></div>公言于帅府，请发众治之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1183779_comment'></div>帅不敢主，使听命于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1183779_comment'></div>公请于朝者三，不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1183779_comment'></div>盖自北虏通好，未尝发众治城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1183779_comment'></div>时韩魏公秉政，使人谕公曰：「城坏，州当自治，何以请为」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1183779_comment'></div>公曰：「役大，法不许擅兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1183779_comment'></div>且完旧，非创筑，何害」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1183779_comment'></div>乃得请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1183779_comment'></div>后数月，始概命诸州治城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1183779_comment'></div>每岁春首，兴役治河，民閒自秋成则为之备，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_71_1183779", 1183779, "Clauses/227/Comments/0")'>贫室</span>尚患不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1183779_comment'></div>是年，二役并兴，人甚苦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1183779_comment'></div>独磁先已毕工，民得复营河役之用，又筑于未冻之前，城得坚固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1183779_comment'></div>迁水部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1183779_comment'></div>神宗即位，覃恩，迁司门郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1183779_comment'></div>是岁，城中瓦屋及濠水上，冰澌盘屈，成花卉之状，奇怪骇目，郡官皆以为嘉瑞，请以上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1183779_comment'></div>公曰：「石晋之末尝有此，朝廷岂不恶之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1183779_comment'></div>众皆服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1183779_comment'></div>代还，知汉州事，迁库部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1183779_comment'></div>蜀俗轻浮，而公临之以安静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1183779_comment'></div>视事之翌日，上谢表，命园中取竹为筒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1183779_comment'></div>众吏持筒走白，杀青而文见于中，曰「君王万岁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1183779_comment'></div>公知其伪，不应，吏惧而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1183779_comment'></div>中元节宴开元寺，盖盛游也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1183779_comment'></div>酒方行，众呼曰：「佛光见」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1183779_comment'></div>观者相腾践，不可禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1183779_comment'></div>公安坐不动，顷之乃定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1183779_comment'></div>大兴州学，亲视敦勉，士人从化者甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1183779_comment'></div>汉守有园圃公田之入，素称优厚，至者无不厚藏而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1183779_comment'></div>公始被命，亲旧以其素贫，皆为之喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1183779_comment'></div>公择而取之，终任所获，布数百匹而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1183779_comment'></div>熙宁中，议行新法，州县嚣然，皆以为不可，公未尝深论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1183779_comment'></div>及法出，为守令者奉行惟恐后，成都一道，抗议指其有未便者，独公一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1183779_comment'></div>时李元瑜为使者，挟朝廷势，凌蔑州郡，沮公以为妄议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1183779_comment'></div>公奏请不俟满罢去，不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1183779_comment'></div>乃移疾，乞授代，不复视事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1183779_comment'></div>归朝，愿就闲局，得管勾西京嵩山崇福宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1183779_comment'></div>岁满再任，迁司农少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1183779_comment'></div>南郊恩，赐金紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1183779_comment'></div>以年及七十，乞致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1183779_comment'></div>家贫口众，仰禄以生，据礼引年，略不以生事为虑，人皆服公勇决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1183779_comment'></div>两经南郊恩，以子叙，迁中散大夫、中大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1183779_comment'></div>今上即位，覃恩，迁太中大夫，累封永年县开国伯，食邑九百户，勋上柱国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1183779_comment'></div>元祐五年正月十三日，以疾终于西京国子监公舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1183779_comment'></div>先居暖室，病革，命迁正寝，享年八十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1183779_comment'></div>太师文彦博、西京留守韩公缜、今左丞苏公颂等九人，相继以公清节言于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1183779_comment'></div>诏赐帛二百匹，仍命有司供其葬事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1183779_comment'></div>以四月十五日，葬于伊川先茔之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1183779_comment'></div>始少师厌五代河北之多乱，徙葬少监于京兆之兴平，将谋居醴泉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1183779_comment'></div>及贵，赐第于泰宁坊，遂再世居京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1183779_comment'></div>嘉祐初，公卜葬祖考于伊川，始居河南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1183779_comment'></div>公娶侯氏，赠尚书比部员外郎道济之女，封寿安县君，先公三十八年终，追封上谷郡君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1183779_comment'></div>男六人：长曰应昌，次曰天锡，皆幼亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1183779_comment'></div>次曰颢，任承议郎、宗正寺丞，先公五年卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1183779_comment'></div>次颐也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1183779_comment'></div>次韩奴，次蛮奴，皆幼亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1183779_comment'></div>女四人：长幼亡，次适奉礼郎席延年，次幼亡，次适都官郎中李正臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1183779_comment'></div>公孝于奉亲，顺于事长，慈于抚幼，宽于治民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1183779_comment'></div>一岁丧母，祖母崔夫人抚爱异于他孙，尝以漆钵贮钱与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1183779_comment'></div>公终身保藏其钵，命子孙宝之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1183779_comment'></div>开府再娶崇国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1183779_comment'></div>时方八岁，已能亲顺颜色，崇国爱之如己出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1183779_comment'></div>奉养五十年，崇国未尝形愠色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1183779_comment'></div>开府喜饮酒，公平生遇美酒，未尝不思亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1183779_comment'></div>颐自垂髫至白首，不记其曾偶忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1183779_comment'></div>遇人与开府同年而生者，士人也无贤愚高下必拜之，贱者亦待之加礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1183779_comment'></div>开府尝从赵炎者贷钱五千，未偿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1183779_comment'></div>公记其姓名，而不知其子孙乡里，终身访求，以不获为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1183779_comment'></div>始公抚育诸孤弟，其长二人仕登朝省，二十馀年閒皆亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1183779_comment'></div>长弟之子九岁，从弟之子十一岁，公复抚养，至于成长，毕其婚宦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1183779_comment'></div>育二孤皆再世，亦异事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1183779_comment'></div>前后五得任子，以均诸父子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1183779_comment'></div>嫁遣孤女，必尽其力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1183779_comment'></div>所得俸钱，分赡亲戚之贫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1183779_comment'></div>伯母刘氏寡居，公奉养甚至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1183779_comment'></div>其女之夫死，公迎从女兄以归，教养其子，均于子侄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1183779_comment'></div>既而女兄之女又寡，公惧女兄之悲思，又取甥女以归，嫁之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1183779_comment'></div>时小官禄薄，克己为义，人以为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1183779_comment'></div>后遇刘氏之族子于襄邑，偶询其宗系，知姻家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1183779_comment'></div>未几刘生卒，其子立之才七岁，公取归教养，今登进士第，为宣德郎矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1183779_comment'></div>公慈恕而刚断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1183779_comment'></div>平居与幼贱语，惟恐有伤其意，至于犯义理，则不假也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1183779_comment'></div>左右使令之人，无日不察其饥饱寒煖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1183779_comment'></div>与人接，淡而有常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1183779_comment'></div>不妄交游，于所信爱，久而益笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1183779_comment'></div>在虔时，常假倅南安军，一狱掾周惇实，年甚少，不为守所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1183779_comment'></div>公视其气貌非常人，与语，果为学知道者，因与为友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1183779_comment'></div>及为郎官，故事当举代，每迁授，辄一荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1183779_comment'></div>闻人有庆乐事，喜之如在己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1183779_comment'></div>不为皎皎之行，平生不亲附权势，而请谒常礼，亦不废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1183779_comment'></div>至于亲旧之贵显者，既不与之加亲，亦不示之疏远，故贤者莫不敬爱，不贤者亦无敢慢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1183779_comment'></div>寓居黄陂时，主簿贪凶人也，常曰：「谚云明镜为丑妇之冤，君居此照我，何其不幸也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1183779_comment'></div>遂颇自敛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1183779_comment'></div>有欧阳乾曜者，以才华自负，多肆轻傲，易公年少，常以语侵公，公如不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1183779_comment'></div>后公官岭下，乾曜适倦道路，公以人船济之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1183779_comment'></div>乾曜曰：「可谓汪汪如千顷之陂也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1183779_comment'></div>南昌黄灏有高才，名动江表，然颇不羁，稠人广坐，无所不狎侮，公时最少，独见礼重，常目公曰：「长者无笑我」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1183779_comment'></div>自少时德度服人已如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1183779_comment'></div>居官临事，孜孜不倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1183779_comment'></div>历守四郡，温恭待下，身率以清慎，所至，寮属无有敢贪纵者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1183779_comment'></div>自朝廷行考课法，无岁不居上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1183779_comment'></div>平生居官，不以私事笞扑人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1183779_comment'></div>公之亲爱者常有所怒，坚请杖之，曰：「吏卒小人，不加以威，是使之慢也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1183779_comment'></div>公曰：「当官用刑，盖假手耳，岂可用于私也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1183779_comment'></div>终不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1183779_comment'></div>谦退不伐善，常欿然自不以为足；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1183779_comment'></div>所能者，虽曲艺小事，人莫知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1183779_comment'></div>平生所为诗甚多，自谓非工，即弃去；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1183779_comment'></div>退休后所作，方稍编录，亦未尝以示人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1183779_comment'></div>自少师以来，家传清白，而公处己尤约，官至四品，奉养如寒士，缣素之衣，有二三十年不易者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1183779_comment'></div>终身非宴会不重肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1183779_comment'></div>既谢事，遂屏朝衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1183779_comment'></div>宾客来者，无贵贱见之，虽公相亦不往谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1183779_comment'></div>方仕宦时，每叹曰：「我贫，未能舍禄仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1183779_comment'></div>茍得早退，休闲十年，志愿足矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1183779_comment'></div>自领崇福，外无职事，内不问家有无者，盖二十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1183779_comment'></div>居常默坐，人问：「静坐既久，宁无闷乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1183779_comment'></div>公笑曰：「吾无闷也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1183779_comment'></div>家人欲其怡悦，每劝之出游，时往亲戚之家，或园亭佛舍，然公之乐不在此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1183779_comment'></div>尝从二子游寿安山，为诗曰：「藏拙归来已十年，身心世事不相关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1183779_comment'></div>洛阳山水寻须遍，更有何人似我闲」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1183779_comment'></div>顾谓二子曰：「游山之乐，犹不如静坐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1183779_comment'></div>盖亦非好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1183779_comment'></div>晚与文潞公、席君从、司马伯康为同甲会，洛中图画，传为盛事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1183779_comment'></div>年八十，丧长子，亲旧以其慈爱素厚，忧不能堪，公以理自处，无过哀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1183779_comment'></div>颐时未仕，阖门皇皇，不知所以为生，公不以为忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1183779_comment'></div>及颐被召，叨备劝讲，人皆庆之，公无甚喜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1183779_comment'></div>尝有疾，召医视脉，曰：「无害」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1183779_comment'></div>公笑曰：「吾年至此矣，有害无害皆可也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1183779_comment'></div>虽疾病，服药必加巾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1183779_comment'></div>年七十，则自为墓志，纪履历始终而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1183779_comment'></div>书其后以戒子孙曰：「吾历官十二任，享禄六十年，但知廉慎宽和，孜孜夙夜，无勋劳可以报国，无异政可以及民，始终得免瑕谪，为幸多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1183779_comment'></div>葬日，切不用干求时贤，制撰铭志，既无事实可纪，不免虚辞溢美，徒累不德，只用此文刻于石，向壁安置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1183779_comment'></div>若或少违遗命，是不以为有知也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1183779_comment'></div>不肖孤奉命不敢违，于葬既无铭，述家传所记，不敢一辞溢美，取诬亲之罪，承公志也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_195_1183779_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1183780' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183780' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183780?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上谷郡君家传</a><span class='authorDate'>（1090年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183780")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183780_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183780'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183780'>先妣夫人姓侯氏，太原盂县人，行第二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183780_comment'></div>世为河东大姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183780_comment'></div>曾祖元，祖皓，当五代之乱，以武勇闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183780_comment'></div>刘氏偏据日，锡土于乌河川，以控寇盗，亡其爵位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183780_comment'></div>父道济，始以儒学中科第，为润州丹徒县令，赠尚书比部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183780_comment'></div>母福昌县太君刁氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183780_comment'></div>夫人幼而聪悟过人，女功之事，无所不能，好读书史，博知古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183780_comment'></div>丹徒君爱之过于子，每以政事问之，所言雅合其意，常叹曰：「恨汝非男子」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183780_comment'></div>七八岁时，常教以古诗曰：「女人不夜出，夜出秉明烛」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183780_comment'></div>自是日暮则不复出房阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183780_comment'></div>刁夫人素有风厥之疾，多夜作，不知人者久之，夫人涕泣扶侍，常连夕不寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183780_comment'></div>年十九，归于我公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183780_comment'></div>事舅姑以孝谨称，与先公相待如宾客，德容之盛，内外亲戚无不敬爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183780_comment'></div>众人游观之所，往往舍所观而观夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183780_comment'></div>先公赖其内助，礼敬尤至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183780_comment'></div>而夫人谦顺自牧，虽小事未尝专，必禀而后行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183780_comment'></div>仁恕宽厚，抚爱诸庶，不异己出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183780_comment'></div>从叔幼孤，夫人存视，常均己子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183780_comment'></div>治家有法，不严而整。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183780_comment'></div>不喜笞扑奴婢，视小臧获如儿女，诸子或加呵责，必戒之曰：「贵贱虽殊，人则一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1183780_comment'></div>汝如此大时，能为此事否」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1183780_comment'></div>道路遗弃小儿，屡收养之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1183780_comment'></div>有小商出未还而其妻死，儿女散逐人去，惟幼者始三岁，人所不取，夫人惧其必死，使抱以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1183780_comment'></div>时聚族甚众，人皆有不欲之色，乃别籴以食之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1183780_comment'></div>其父归，谢曰：「幸蒙收养，得全其生，愿以为献」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1183780_comment'></div>夫人曰：「我本以待汝归，非欲之也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1183780_comment'></div>好为药饵，以济病者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1183780_comment'></div>大寒，有负炭而𢶡者过门，家人欲呼之，夫人劝止之曰：「慎勿为此，胜则贫者困矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1183780_comment'></div>先公凡有所怒，必为之宽解，唯诸儿有过则不掩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1183780_comment'></div>常曰：「子之所以不肖者，由母蔽其过而父不知也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1183780_comment'></div>夫人男子六人，所存惟二，其爱慈可谓至矣，然于教之之道，不少假也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1183780_comment'></div>才数岁，行而或踣，家人走前扶抱，恐其惊啼，夫人未尝不呵责曰：「汝若安徐，宁至踣乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1183780_comment'></div>饮食常置之坐侧，尝食絮羹，皆叱止之，曰：「幼求称欲，长当如何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1183780_comment'></div>虽使令辈，不得以恶言骂之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1183780_comment'></div>故颐兄弟平生于饮食衣服无所择，不能恶言骂人，非性然也，教之使然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1183780_comment'></div>与人争忿，虽直不右，曰：「患其不能屈，不患其不能伸」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1183780_comment'></div>及稍长，常使从善师友游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1183780_comment'></div>虽居贫，或欲延客，则喜而为之具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1183780_comment'></div>其教女，常以曹大家《女戒》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1183780_comment'></div>居常教告家人曰：「见人善，则当如己善，必共成之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1183780_comment'></div>视他物，当如己物，必加爱之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1183780_comment'></div>先公罢尉庐陵，赴调，寓居历阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1183780_comment'></div>会叔父亦解掾毗陵，聚口甚众，储备不足，夫人经营转易，得不困乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1183780_comment'></div>先公归，问其所为，叹曰：「良转运使才也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1183780_comment'></div>所居之处，邻妇里姥皆愿为之用，虽劳不怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1183780_comment'></div>始寓丹阳，僦葛氏舍以居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1183780_comment'></div>守舍王氏翁姥庸狡，前后居者无不苦之，夫人待之有道，遂反柔良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1183780_comment'></div>及迁去，王姥涕恋不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1183780_comment'></div>夫人安于贫约，服用俭素，观亲族间纷华相尚，如无所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1183780_comment'></div>少女方数岁，忽失所在，乳姥辈悲泣叫号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1183780_comment'></div>夫人骂止之，曰：「在当求得，茍亡失矣，汝如是将何为」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1183780_comment'></div>在庐陵时，公宇多怪，家人告曰：「物弄扇」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1183780_comment'></div>夫人曰：「热尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1183780_comment'></div>又曰：「物击鼓」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1183780_comment'></div>夫人曰：「有椎乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1183780_comment'></div>可与之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1183780_comment'></div>后家人不敢复言怪，怪亦不复有，遂获安居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1183780_comment'></div>夫人有知人之鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1183780_comment'></div>姜应明者，中神童第，人竞观之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1183780_comment'></div>夫人曰：「非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_59_1183780", 1183780, "Clauses/196/Comments/2")'>远器</span>也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1183780_comment'></div>后果以罪废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1183780_comment'></div>颐兄弟幼时，夫人勉之读书，因书线贴上曰「我惜勤读书儿」，又并书二行，曰「殿前及第程延寿」，先兄幼时名也，次曰「处士」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1183780_comment'></div>及先兄登第，颐以不才罢应科举，方知夫人知之于童稚中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1183780_comment'></div>宝藏手泽，使后世子孙知夫人之精鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1183780_comment'></div>夫人好文，而不为辞章，见世之妇女以文章笔札传于人者，深以为非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1183780_comment'></div>平生所为诗，不过三十篇，皆不存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1183780_comment'></div>独记在历阳时，先公觐亲河朔，夜闻鸣雁，尝为诗曰：「何处惊飞起？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1183780_comment'></div>雍雍过草堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1183780_comment'></div>早是愁无寐，忽闻意转伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1183780_comment'></div>良人沙塞外，羁妾守空房。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1183780_comment'></div>欲寄回文信，谁能付汝将」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1183780_comment'></div>读史，见奸邪逆乱之事，常掩卷愤叹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1183780_comment'></div>见忠孝节义之士，则钦慕不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1183780_comment'></div>尝称唐太宗得御戎之道，其识虑高远，有英雄之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1183780_comment'></div>夫人之弟可世称名儒，才智甚高，尝自谓不如夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1183780_comment'></div>夫人自少多病，好方饵修养之术，甚得其效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1183780_comment'></div>从先公官岭外，偶迎凉露寝，遂中瘴疠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1183780_comment'></div>及北归，道中病革，召医视脉，曰可治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1183780_comment'></div>谓二子曰：「绐尔也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1183780_comment'></div>未终前一日，命颐曰：「今日百五，为我祀父母，明年不复祀矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1183780_comment'></div>夫人以景德元年甲辰十月十三日，生于太原；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1183780_comment'></div>皇祐四年壬辰二月二十八日，终于江宁，享年四十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1183780_comment'></div>始封寿安县君，追封上谷郡君。</div><div id='poem_sentence_82_1183780_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年</a>　葬父，使周行己主客。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年</a>　尹焞问学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年</a>　鲍若雨、刘安世、刘安节数人来洛问学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年</a>　郭忠孝问《论语》<br /></div><div class='label1' id='053692b1242b452ab8a623ff77d07519_label'><a href='javascript:
