ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年</a>　尹焞从程颐学《易》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年</a>　除直秘阁判西京国子监，辞。作品：河南府，西京。免判国子监状。<div id='poem_1183681' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183681' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183681?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免服除直秘阁判西京国子监状</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐七年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183681")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183681_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183681'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183681'>臣今月一日，准河南府差人送到官诰一道，伏蒙圣恩，授臣左通直郎、直秘阁、权判西京国子监者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183681_comment'></div>臣昨被责命，出为外官，夙夜靡遑，惟是内省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183681_comment'></div>始蒙招致之礼，旋为黜逐之人，将胡颜以立朝，当自劾而引去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183681_comment'></div>至于五请而未听，岂可力辩以求伸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183681_comment'></div>遂且从容，以须替罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183681_comment'></div>未及任满，遽丁家艰，思无忝于所生，惟坚持于素节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183681_comment'></div>未终丧制，已降除书，上体眷恩，内深愧惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183681_comment'></div>伏念臣志存守道，识昧随时，俗所忌憎，动招谤毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183681_comment'></div>昨蒙擢任，既以人言被黜，为朝廷羞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183681_comment'></div>今复授以职任，适足重为朝廷羞，无所益于明时，徒取笑于后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183681_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，矜察愚诚，追寝恩命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183681_comment'></div>臣昨因丁忧既已去官，今来所降诰命，不敢祗受，已于河南府寄纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183681_comment'></div>伏乞朝廷检会臣前来五次奏陈，特赐指挥，许归田里。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1183681_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年4月</a>　除直秘阁判西京国子监，再辞。作品：再辞免状。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年4月</a>　范祖禹为程颐辩白本末。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年4月</a>　论立孟后诏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年5月</a>　监察御史董敦逸奏程颐有怨望轻躁语。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年</a>　改授管勾崇福宫。作品：谢管勾崇福宫状。<div id='poem_1183683' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183683' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183683?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢管勾崇福宫状</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐七年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183683")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183683_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183683'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183683'>臣昨蒙圣恩，除臣左通直郎、直秘阁、权判西京国子监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183683_comment'></div>两具表状辞免，乞归田里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183683_comment'></div>今月十日，准敕特授左通直郎、管勾西京嵩山崇福宫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183683_comment'></div>误蒙甄录，再露封章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183683_comment'></div>不敢逊言，惟尽敬主之意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183683_comment'></div>深陈古义，盖存报国之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183683_comment'></div>天听至高，言已尽而诚孚未格；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183683_comment'></div>君威难犯，虑其渎而忧惧交深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183683_comment'></div>非特畏于刑章，实愿存于国体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183683_comment'></div>幸蒙宽贷，岂敢频烦？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183683_comment'></div>臣更不敢固违朝命，所降敕牒，臣已领讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183683_comment'></div>伏为见患腰跨，拜受未得，候痊损日，谢恩就职次。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1183683_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年8月</a>　申河南府寻医。作品：乞寻医状。<div id='poem_1183684' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183684' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183684?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申河南府乞寻医状</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐七年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183684")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183684_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183684'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183684'>颐昨准敕授左通直郎、管勾嵩山崇福宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183684_comment'></div>寻具奏闻，为患腰跨，拜授未得，候痊损日，谢恩就职次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183684_comment'></div>今来已满百日，未得痊安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183684_comment'></div>窃惧久稽朝命，欲乞寻医，谨具申西京留府，伏乞依条施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1183684_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年9月</a>　哲宗初亲政，申秘阁西监，再辞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年</a>　吕大防推荐其为馆职，坚辞不受；又以百缣赠，辞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年</a>　苗履来问学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年5月</a>　杨时以师礼拜见程颐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年</a>　杨时、游酢来问学，程门立雪。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　居洛，杨应之卒，有祭文。作品：祭杨应之文。<div id='poem_1183790' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183790' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183790?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭杨应之文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183790")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183790_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183790'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183790'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183790_comment'></div>昔予与君，邂逅相遇于大江之南，言契气合，遂从予游，岁将三纪，情均骨肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183790_comment'></div>忽闻来讣，何痛如之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183790_comment'></div>呜呼应之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183790_comment'></div>谁谓君而止于此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183790_comment'></div>高才伟度，绝出群类；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183790_comment'></div>善志奇蕴，曾未得施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183790_comment'></div>天胡为厚其禀而啬其年？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183790_comment'></div>人谁不死，君之死为可恨也，奚止交旧之情，悲哀而已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183790_comment'></div>管城之原，归祔先兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183790_comment'></div>属予衰年，惮于长道，不能临穴一恸，以伸余情，姑致菲薄之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183790_comment'></div>魂兮其来，歆此诚意！</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1183790_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年3月30日</a>　居洛，朱光庭卒，有祭文。作品：祭朱公掞文。<div id='poem_1183791' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183791' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183791?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭朱公掞文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年3月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183791")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183791_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183791'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183791'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183791_comment'></div>道既不明，世罕信者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183791_comment'></div>不信则不求，不求则何得？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183791_comment'></div>斯道之所以久不明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183791_comment'></div>自予兄弟倡学之初，众方惊异，君时甚少，独信不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183791_comment'></div>非夫豪杰特立之士，能如是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183791_comment'></div>笃学力行，至于没齿，志不渝于金石，行可质于神明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183791_comment'></div>在邦在家，临民临事，造次动静，一由至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183791_comment'></div>上论古人，岂易其比？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183791_comment'></div>蹇蹇王臣之节，凛凛循吏之风，著见事为，皆可纪述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183791_comment'></div>谓当大施于时，必得其寿，天胡难忱，遽止于此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183791_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183791_comment'></div>不幸七八年之间，同志共学之人，相继而逝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183791_comment'></div>今君复往，使予踽踽于世，忧道学之寡助，则予之哭君，岂特交朋之情而已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183791_comment'></div>邙山之阳，归祔先宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183791_comment'></div>思平生之深契，痛音容之永隔，陈薄奠以将诚，庶英灵兮来格！</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1183791_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年3月</a>　李清臣主礼部试，黜元祐之政，尹焞不对而出，归告其母，其母许之。程颐称赞其母贤德。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　章惇为相，欲起用邵伯温，伯温拒赴。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年9月</a>　居洛，阅故编，思念吕大临。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　居洛，专研学问，编成《六礼》作品：《礼》序。<div id='poem_1183744' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183744' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183744?labeling=true' target='_blank'>礼序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1095年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183744")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183744_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183744'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183744'>礼经三百，威仪三千，皆出于性，非伪貌饰情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183744_comment'></div>鄙夫野人卒然加敬，逡巡逊却而不敢受；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183744_comment'></div>三尺童子拱而趋市，暴夫悍卒莫敢狎焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183744_comment'></div>彼非素有于教与邀誉于人而然也，盖其所有于性，物感而出者如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183744_comment'></div>故天尊地卑，礼固立矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183744_comment'></div>类聚群分，礼固行矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183744_comment'></div>人者，位乎天地之间，立乎万物之上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183744_comment'></div>天地与吾同体，万物与吾同气，尊卑分类，不设而彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183744_comment'></div>圣人循此，制为冠、昏、丧、祭、朝、聘、射、飨之礼，以行君臣、父子、兄弟、夫妇、朋友之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183744_comment'></div>其形而下者，具于饮食器服之用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183744_comment'></div>其形而上者，极于无声无臭之微；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183744_comment'></div>众人勉之，贤人行之，圣人由之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183744_comment'></div>故所以行其身与其家与其国与其天下，礼治则治，礼乱则乱，礼存则存，礼亡则亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183744_comment'></div>上自古始，下逮五季，质文不同，罔不由是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183744_comment'></div>然而世有损益，惟周为备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183744_comment'></div>是以夫子尝曰：「郁郁乎文哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183744_comment'></div>吾从周」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183744_comment'></div>逮其弊也，忠义之薄，情文之繁，林放有礼本之问，而孔子欲先进之从，盖所以矫正反弊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183744_comment'></div>然岂礼之过哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183744_comment'></div>为礼者之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1183744_comment'></div>秦氏焚灭典籍，三代礼文大坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1183744_comment'></div>汉兴购书，《礼记》四十九篇杂出诸儒传记，不能悉得圣人之旨，考其文义，时有牴牾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1183744_comment'></div>然而其文繁，其义博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1183744_comment'></div>学者观之，如适大通之肆，珠珍器帛随其所取；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1183744_comment'></div>如游阿房之宫，千门万户随其所入；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1183744_comment'></div>博而约之，亦可以弗畔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1183744_comment'></div>盖其说也，粗在应对进退之间，而精在道德性命之要；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1183744_comment'></div>始于童幼之习，而终于圣人之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1183744_comment'></div>惟达于道者，然后能知其言，能知其言，然后能得于礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1183744_comment'></div>然则礼之所以为礼，其则不远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1183744_comment'></div>昔者颜子之所从事，不出乎视听言动之间，而《乡党》之记孔子，多在于动容周旋之际，此学者所当致疑以思，致思以达也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1183744_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='dcfe7c9aaf3e4818bbf8dd2facaa038c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dcfe7c9aaf3e4818bbf8dd2facaa038c");'><span id='dcfe7c9aaf3e4818bbf8dd2facaa038c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1097')">1096-1097年</a>，64-65岁</div><div id='dcfe7c9aaf3e4818bbf8dd2facaa038c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　居洛，答杨时书。作品：答杨中立论《西铭》书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年2月</a>　追毁出身以来文字，放归田里。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年6月</a>　叔父程珫卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年10月</a>　葬叔父程珫于伊川先茔，作墓志铭。作品：程珫墓志铭。<div id='poem_1183783' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183783' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183783?labeling=true' target='_blank'>叔父朝奉墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183783")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183783_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183783'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183783'>叔父名珫，字季聪，赠太子少师讳羽、清河郡太君张氏、襄陵郡太君贾氏之曾孙，尚书虞部员外郎讳希振、高密县君崔氏之孙，赠开府仪同三司讳遹、荣国太夫人张氏、崇国太夫张氏之子，先公太中之季弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183783_comment'></div>其上世居深州之博野，累代聚居，以孝义称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183783_comment'></div>至少师显于朝，赐第京师，始居开封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183783_comment'></div>先君葬祖考于伊川，遂迁河南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183783_comment'></div>公天性孝友淳质，不事文饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183783_comment'></div>幼孤，事崇国能竭其力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183783_comment'></div>于宗族笃恩义，爱幼稚如己生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183783_comment'></div>事伯兄丘嫂如父母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183783_comment'></div>与人接，倾尽心腑，信人如己，屡致欺而不变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183783_comment'></div>人多笑之，而好德者重之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183783_comment'></div>年四十五，始以伯兄太中恩，补郊社斋郎，调怀州修武县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183783_comment'></div>秩满，授权泽州端氏县令，阅岁即真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183783_comment'></div>用荐者，改大理寺丞，复四迁，至朝奉郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183783_comment'></div>积勋至上轻车都尉，赐服银绯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183783_comment'></div>历河中府龙门、汝州襄城县事，权管勾西京国子监，遂致官事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183783_comment'></div>公当官竭力，不择难易，尽心于爱人，故所至民爱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183783_comment'></div>尝捕蝗，徒步执彗，为众人先，其不爱力皆此类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183783_comment'></div>喜求民利病，力可行者行之，不能者言之上官，虽沮却不恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183783_comment'></div>年五十始有子，伤从兄无嗣，遂以继之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183783_comment'></div>先君六得任子恩，公与二子实居其三，则公之见爱于兄，与先君之厚于弟，可见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1183783_comment'></div>娶贾氏，追封宜兴县君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1183783_comment'></div>继室张氏，封寿光县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1183783_comment'></div>子二人：长曰頔，郊社斋郎，出继从伯父后；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1183783_comment'></div>次曰颙，太庙斋郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1183783_comment'></div>女二人：长适承议郎刘立之，次适进士王霂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1183783_comment'></div>公生于天圣元年四月壬寅，终于绍圣四年六月乙酉，历年七十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1183783_comment'></div>是年十月某日，葬于伊川，祔先茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1183783_comment'></div>孤侄颐号泣而铭其穴曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1183783'>孝于事亲，顺于事兄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1183783_comment'></div>质直而好义，勤瘁以奉公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1183783_comment'></div>家无间言，仕有善效，古之所谓躬行君子，公其是乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1183783_comment'></div>归全于斯，呜呼哀哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1183783_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='457365c170e24386973e882276f1f594_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("457365c170e24386973e882276f1f594");'><span id='457365c170e24386973e882276f1f594_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1107')">1100-1107年</a>，68-75岁</div><div id='457365c170e24386973e882276f1f594' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　张绎来从学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　孟厚来从学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年10月</a>　复通直郎，权判西京国子监。作品：谢复官表。<div id='poem_1183687' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183687' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183687?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢复官表</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183687")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183687_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183687'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183687'>臣颐言：今月二十日，准河南府送到官诰一道，伏蒙圣恩，授臣通直郎、权判西京国子监者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183687_comment'></div>始窜遐荒，分甘终废；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183687_comment'></div>岂期洪造，复畀旧官？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183687_comment'></div>仰荷恩私，伏增愧惧<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183687_comment'></div>窃念臣天资愚暗，自致放投；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183687_comment'></div>既仰荷于宽恩，如安居于乐土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183687_comment'></div>忽遇非常之宥，继蒙牵复之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183687_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下道大兼容，明无不照，念先帝经筵之旧，推至仁爱物之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183687_comment'></div>臣敢不益善其身，励精所学，期有传于后世，以上报于深恩！</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1183687_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年12月</a>　提举京西路常平公事方宙请还先生田徒，不果。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　与侯仲良论人才使用。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　罗从彦至洛从学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年5月</a>　追所复官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　居洛，谢良佐来问学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　居洛，张绎来请学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　归洛，易传已成；晁说之来求学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年5月8日</a>　入元祐党籍，居伊川。作品：答周孚先问。<div id='poem_1183716' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183716' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183716?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答周孚先问<span class='inlineComment2'>（并跋）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年5月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183716")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183716_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183716'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183716'>问：先生旧语门人云：「天下至忙者，无如禅客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183716_comment'></div>市井之人，虽曰营利，犹有休息时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183716_comment'></div>禅客行住坐卧，无不在道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183716_comment'></div>存无不在道之心，便是至忙」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183716_comment'></div>孚先窃谓此语如孟子所谓「必有事焉而勿正，心勿忘勿助长」也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183716_comment'></div>若正若助长，即是忙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183716_comment'></div>或者谓此语非为学者设，谓以圣人方之禅客未尝闲，若学者须是行住坐卧在道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183716_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1183716'>存无不在道之心，便是助长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183716_comment'></div>方其学也，固当有事，亦当知助长之非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183716_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1183716'>问：《书》曰：「惟圣罔念作狂，惟狂克念作圣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183716_comment'></div>孚先窃谓，圣者谓有圣人资质，一不念则流入于狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183716_comment'></div>狂者进取，曾晰之徒是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183716_comment'></div>借如颜子，不能拳拳服膺，亦必至于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183716_comment'></div>若是圣人，则从心所欲不踰矩，虽不念亦无害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183716_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1183716'>六德：知仁圣义中和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183716_comment'></div>圣，通明之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183716_comment'></div>狂，狂愚之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183716_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1183716'>问：孔子曰：「知者乐水，仁者<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1183716", 1183716, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>乐山</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183716_comment'></div>知者动，仁者静；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183716_comment'></div>知者乐，仁者寿」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1183716_comment'></div>孚先窃谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1183716", 1183716, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>乐山</span>乐水状仁知之体，动静述仁知之用，乐与寿明仁知之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1183716_comment'></div>知则能知之，能知之则务穷物理，务穷物理则运用不息，故乐水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1183716_comment'></div>水谓其周流也，故动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1183716_comment'></div>动谓其理之无穷也，故乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1183716_comment'></div>乐谓其无疑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1183716_comment'></div>仁则能体之，能体之则有得于所性，有得于所性则循理而行之，故<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1183716", 1183716, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>乐山</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1183716_comment'></div>山谓其安止也，故静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1183716_comment'></div>静谓其无待于外也，故寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1183716_comment'></div>寿谓其达生理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1183716_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1183716'>言意未能体仁知，且宜潜思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1183716_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1183716'>问：孔子曰：「知及之，仁不能守之，虽得之，必失之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1183716_comment'></div>知及之，仁能守之，不庄以涖之，则民不敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1183716_comment'></div>知及之，仁能守之，庄以涖之，动之不以礼，未善也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1183716_comment'></div>孚先窃谓，此语是告学者，亦是入道之序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1183716_comment'></div>故知及之者，见得到也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1183716_comment'></div>仁能守之者，孳孳于此也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1183716_comment'></div>庄以涖之者，外设藩垣以远暴慢也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1183716_comment'></div>动之以礼，观时应用皆欲中节也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1183716_comment'></div>或者谓此是人君事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1183716_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1183716'>临政处己，莫不皆然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1183716_comment'></div>所谓仁能守之者，孳孳于此也，此言未能尽仁，且宜致思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1183716_comment'></div>仁则安矣，所以云守也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1183716_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_1183716'>孚先旧讲习太学，建中靖国庚辰冬，过洛阳，游伊川先生之门，预群弟子之列，亲炙模范，时闻诲语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1183716_comment'></div>越明年暮春，归省庭闱，期岁复入学，以所疑为书，请质于先生，皆得亲笔开谕，逮今几四十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1183716_comment'></div>以今日视前日，固知学之不博，问之不切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1183716_comment'></div>日月逝矣，功不加倍，只益自歉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1183716_comment'></div>绍兴丁巳冬，周孚先谨书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1183716_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　居伊川，作答学者书。作品：答张宏中书。<div id='poem_1183717' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183717' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183717?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答张闳中书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183717")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183717_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183717'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183717'>《易传》未传，自量精力未衰，尚觊有少进尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183717_comment'></div>然亦不必直待身后，觉耄则传矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183717_comment'></div>书虽未出，学未尝不传也，第患无受之者尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183717_comment'></div>来书云：「《易》之义本起于数」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183717_comment'></div>谓义起于数则非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183717_comment'></div>有理而后有象，有象而后有数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183717_comment'></div>《易》因象以明理，由象而知数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183717_comment'></div>得其义，则象数在其中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183717_comment'></div>必欲穷象之隐微，尽数之毫忽，乃寻流逐末，术家之所尚，非儒者之所务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183717_comment'></div>管辂、郭璞之徒是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183717_comment'></div>理无形也，故因象以明理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183717_comment'></div>理既见乎辞矣，则可由辞以观象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183717_comment'></div>故曰：得其义，则象数在其中矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1183717_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　居伊川，作答弟子书。作品：答杨时书。<div id='poem_1183718' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183718' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183718?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答杨时书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183718")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183718_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183718'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183718'>颐启：相别多年，常深渴想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183718_comment'></div>前日自伊川归，得十一月十五日南康发来书，知赴新任，体况安佳，甚慰远怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183718_comment'></div>颐如常，自去冬来，多在伊川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183718_comment'></div>见谋居伊，力薄未能遽成耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183718_comment'></div>朝廷设教官，盖欲教人修身齐家治国平天下之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183718_comment'></div>茍能修职，则「不素餐兮」，孰大于是？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183718_comment'></div>赴省试令子，不知其名，中第可喻及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183718_comment'></div>名迪者好学质美，当成远器，应未有北来期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183718_comment'></div>两小子<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>承问，故及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183718_comment'></div>此独与诸孙处，岁计稔则自馀，无足道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183718_comment'></div>春暄，惟进学自爱，不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183718_comment'></div>颐启杨君教授。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1183718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1183718'><span class='label'>按：</span>三月六日。<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_8_1183718_0'>⑴ 大者项城尉，小者鄢陵尉。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1183718_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　居伊川，作答学者书。作品：答杨迪书。<div id='poem_1183719' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183719' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183719?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答杨迪书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183719")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183719_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183719'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183719'>相别累月，思渴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183719_comment'></div>前承惠书，恐已出京，故不复奉答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183719_comment'></div>近又收书，乃知未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183719_comment'></div>喜闻夏暑安佳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183719_comment'></div>前书所问心迹之说，固知未能无疑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183719_comment'></div>若以心迹有判，则象忧亦忧，乃伪矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183719_comment'></div>是宜精索，未易晓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183719_comment'></div>又云：「有道，又有易，何如」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183719_comment'></div>此语全未是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183719_comment'></div>更将《传序》详思，当自通矣<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183719_comment'></div>大率所论，辞与意太多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183719_comment'></div>孔、孟之门人，岂能尽与孔、孟同？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183719_comment'></div>唯其不敢信己而信其师之说，是以能思而卒同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183719_comment'></div>若纷然致疑，终亦必亡而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183719_comment'></div>勉之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183719_comment'></div>勉之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183719_comment'></div>盛暑在途，千百自爱。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1183719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1183719'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_1183719_0'>⑴ 变易而后合道，易字与道字不相似也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1183719_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　居伊川，作答门人书。<div id='poem_1183720' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183720' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183720?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答门人书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183720")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183720_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183720'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183720'>前者奉答，适病倦不能详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183720_comment'></div>后来亲知讲论，几盈箱矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183720_comment'></div>设端虽多，大率意不相远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183720_comment'></div>于大概尚弗识，况屈伸久速之际乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183720_comment'></div>平日不谓至如是，岂皆知不足以及之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183720_comment'></div>盖为众说漂煦，不能自立尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183720_comment'></div>此由见信不笃故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183720_comment'></div>孔、孟之门岂皆贤哲？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183720_comment'></div>固多众人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183720_comment'></div>以众人观圣贤，弗识者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183720_comment'></div>惟其不敢信己而信其师，是故求而后得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183720_comment'></div>今诸君于颐言，才不合则置不复思，所以终异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183720_comment'></div>不可便放下，更且思之，致知之方也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183720_comment'></div>姑求自晓，无庸他恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183720_comment'></div>深尤不知者，甚无谓也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1183720_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　在伊川，同弟子门生切磋学问。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　居伊川，作答学者书。作品：答鲍若雨书。<div id='poem_1183721' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183721' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183721?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答鲍若雨书并答问</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183721")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183721_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183721'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183721'>颐咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183721_comment'></div>诸君处，常问知动止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183721_comment'></div>忽领惠书，审已安康，其慰可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183721_comment'></div>颐如常，不烦见念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183721_comment'></div>示及所疑，百忙中谢君告行，不暇周悉，略奉答，思之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183721_comment'></div>袢暑，千百善爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183721_comment'></div>五月十日，颐咨鲍君秀才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183721_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1183721'>疑难六，谨写拜呈，伏乞详赐指谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183721_comment'></div>若雨拜覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183721_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1183721'>佛氏轮回之说，凡为善者死，则复生为善人，为恶者死，则变而为禽兽之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183721_comment'></div>虽无此实应，窃恐有此理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183721_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183721_comment'></div>凡禀冲气以生者，未始不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183721_comment'></div>圣人先得人之所同者而践履之，故能保全太和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183721_comment'></div>至死，其气冥会于中和之所，造化之中，自然有复生为人之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183721_comment'></div>愚者平居作恶，而冲气已丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183721_comment'></div>至死，其气则会于缪戾之所，造化之中，自然有为禽兽之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183721_comment'></div>故曰恐有此理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183721_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1183721'>夫子曰：「未知生，焉知死」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183721_comment'></div>知生则知死矣，能原始则能要终矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1183721_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1183721'>《易》曰：「阴阳不测之谓神」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1183721_comment'></div>又曰：「神妙万物而为言」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1183721_comment'></div>观此，则佛氏所谓鬼神者妄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1183721_comment'></div>然「祖考来格」，「敬鬼神而远之」之说，则似乎有佛氏所谓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1183721_comment'></div>意者，气类感应处，便是来格，但当致诚，不当亵近，近得却有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1183721_comment'></div>不知此说如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1183721_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1183721'>潜心久当自明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1183721_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1183721'>孟子曰：「其为气也，至大至刚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1183721_comment'></div>以直养而无害，则塞于天地之閒」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1183721_comment'></div>尝谓凡人气量窄狭，只为私心隔断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1183721_comment'></div>茍以直养而无害，则无私心，茍无私心，则志气自然广大，充塞于天地之閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1183721_comment'></div>气象有可以意会而莫能状者，此所谓难言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1183721_comment'></div>或谓塞于天地之閒，只是到处去得，此言似无气味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1183721_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1183721'>如是涵养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1183721_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1183721'>乐正子见孟子，孟子曰：「子亦来见我乎<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云。）</span>」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1183721_comment'></div>观此一篇，都无圣人气象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1183721_comment'></div>或谓乐正子从子敖，有激而云，不得不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1183721_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_1183721'>此无疑，真孟子之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1183721_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1183721'>「今之成人者何必然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1183721_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1183721", 1183721, "Clauses/95/Comments/0")'>见利思义</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1183721", 1183721, "Clauses/96/Comments/0")'>见危授命</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1183721", 1183721, "Clauses/97/Comments/0")'>久要</span>不忘<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1183721", 1183721, "Clauses/97/Comments/1")'>平生</span>之言，亦可以为成人矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1183721_comment'></div>此言是子路说耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1183721_comment'></div>孔子说耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1183721_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_1183721'>仲尼言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1183721_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1183721'>孟子曰：「不孝有三，无后为大」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1183721_comment'></div>所谓二不孝何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1183721_comment'></div>说者谓陷父于不义，与家贫亲老，不求禄仕，窃恐不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1183721_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1183721'>何以知不然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1183721_comment'></div>所谓禄仕，凡所以养皆同。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1183721_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　在伊川，谢湜来问学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　在伊川，吕好问来问学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年2月</a>　作印铭，有序。作品：印铭序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年4月30日</a>　追毁出身以来文字。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年4月</a>　作《春秋传》序。作品：春秋传序。<div id='poem_1183735' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183735' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183735?labeling=true' target='_blank'>春秋传序<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁二年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183735")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183735_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183735'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183735'>天之生民，必有出类之才起而君长之，治之而争夺息，导之而生养遂，教之而伦理明，然后人道立，天道成，地道平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183735_comment'></div>二帝而上，圣贤世出，随时有作，顺乎风气之宜，不先天以开人，各因时而立政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183735_comment'></div>暨乎三王迭兴，三重既备，子丑寅之建正，忠质文之更尚，人道备矣，天运周矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183735_comment'></div>圣王既不复作，有天下者虽欲仿古之迹，亦私意妄为而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183735_comment'></div>事之谬，秦至以建亥为正；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183735_comment'></div>道之悖，汉专以智力持世，岂复知先王之道也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183735_comment'></div>夫子当周之末，以圣人不复作也，顺天应时之治不复有也，于是作《春秋》，为百王不易之大法，所谓考诸三王而不谬，建诸天地而不悖，质诸鬼神而无疑，百世以俟圣人而不惑者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183735_comment'></div>先儒之《传》曰：「游、夏不能赞一辞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183735_comment'></div>辞不待赞也，言不能与于斯耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183735_comment'></div>斯道也，惟颜子尝闻之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183735_comment'></div>「行夏之时，乘殷之辂，服周之冕，乐则《韶》舞」，此其准的也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183735_comment'></div>后世以史视《春秋》，谓褒善贬恶而已，至于经世之大法则不知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183735_comment'></div>《春秋》大义数十，其义虽大，炳如日星，乃易见也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183735_comment'></div>惟其微辞隐义，时措从宜者为难知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183735_comment'></div>或抑或纵，或与或夺，或进或退，或微或显，而得乎义理之安，文质之中，宽猛之宜，是非之公，乃制事之权衡，揆道之模范也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183735_comment'></div>夫观百物，然后识化工之神；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183735_comment'></div>聚众材，然后知作室之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183735_comment'></div>于一事一义而欲窥圣人之用心，非上智不能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183735_comment'></div>故学《春秋》者，必优游涵泳，默识心通，然后能造其微也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183735_comment'></div>后王知《春秋》之义，则虽德非禹、汤，尚可以法三代之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1183735_comment'></div>自秦而下，其学不传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1183735_comment'></div>予悼夫圣人之志不明于后世也，故作《传》以明之，俾后之人通其文而求其义，得其意而法其用，则三代可复也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1183735_comment'></div>是《传》也，虽未能极圣人之蕴奥，庶几学者得其门而入矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1183735_comment'></div>有宋崇宁二年癸未四月乙亥，伊川程颐序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1183735_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>　王蘋问学于程颐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年7月</a>　禁元祐学术政事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年8月</a>　颁党人姓名，程颐于余官为二十三人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年11月4日</a>　言者论程颐聚徒传授，乞禁绝；迁居龙门之南，止四方学者。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年11月8日</a>　范致虚知河南府，实施禁学行动。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　陈贵一问学于程颐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　程颐论诗大序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　李邦直卒，有祭文。作品：祭李邦直文。<div id='poem_1183796' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183796' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183796?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭李邦直文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183796")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183796_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183796'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183796'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183796_comment'></div>惟公世推文章，位登丞辅，简编见其才华，廊庙存其步武，固不待诔而后知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183796_comment'></div>自与公别，于兹九年，既升沉之异迹，望履舄以无缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183796_comment'></div>惟期与公挂冠之后，居洛之滨，葛巾藜杖，日以相亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183796_comment'></div>何志愿之未谐，遂音容之永隔！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183796_comment'></div>追念平昔，悲辛填臆，呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183796_comment'></div>颐也少服公名，晚识公面，重以姻媾，始终异眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183796_comment'></div>感怀知遇，丹诚莫见，一恸灵筵，聊伸薄奠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1183796_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年1月</a>　以星变毁元祐党人碑，程颐复承务郎依旧致仕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年3月</a>　以通直郎致仕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年</a>　得风痹疾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　风痹疾小愈，尹焞视疾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年9月17日</a>　卒于家中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　葬洛，弟子作文悼念。作品：祭文。祭文。祭文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　葬洛，邵溥素衣白马视之。<br -----title
扶沟
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b42bfb1d9ce440688fd76abf71949f23_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b42bfb1d9ce440688fd76abf71949f23");'><span id='b42bfb1d9ce440688fd76abf71949f23_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1079')">1078-1079年</a>，46-47岁</div><div id='b42bfb1d9ce440688fd76abf71949f23' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年</a>　兄程颢知扶沟县事，程颐侍行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年</a>　谢良佐将归应举，程颐与之论道。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年</a>　以事至京师，称赞游酢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年</a>　以事至京师，程颐与兄程颢以倡明道学为己任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年1月</a>　西斋南窗下书三十年前所作养鱼记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年3月</a>　作禊饮诗序。<div id='poem_1183736' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183736' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183736?labeling=true' target='_blank'>禊饮诗序<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1079年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183736")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183736_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183736'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183736'>上巳禊饮，风流远矣，而兰亭之会，最为后人所称慕者，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183736_comment'></div>盖其游多豪逸之才，而右军之书，复为好事者所重尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183736_comment'></div>事之显晦，未尝不在人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183736_comment'></div>颍川陈公廙始治洛居，则引流回环，为泛觞之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183736_comment'></div>元丰己未，首修禊事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183736_comment'></div>公廙好古重道，所会皆儒学之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183736_comment'></div>既乐嘉宾，形于咏歌，有不愧山阴之句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183736_comment'></div>诸君属而和者，皆有高致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183736_comment'></div>野人程颐不能赋诗，因论今昔之异，而为之评曰：以好贤方逐乐之心，礼义为疏旷之比，道艺当笔札之功，诚不愧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183736_comment'></div>安知后日之视今日，不若今人之慕昔人也哉？</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1183736_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年</a>　作上富郑公书。<div id='poem_1183699' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183699' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183699?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上富郑公书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1079年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183699")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183699_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183699'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183699'>伊川程颐斋心裁书，再拜献于致政司空相公阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183699_comment'></div>颐鄙野之人，未尝请谒有位，故不获从乡里士子趋进门下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183699_comment'></div>今者来自山中，闻太皇太后厌代，心诚有所迫切，无路上达，敢以闻于左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183699_comment'></div>盖非公无可告者，非公无肯为者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183699_comment'></div>颐顷岁见治昭陵，制度规画，一出匠者之拙谋，中人之私意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183699_comment'></div>宰执而下，受成而已，莫复置思，以巨木架石为之屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183699_comment'></div>计不百年，必当损坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183699_comment'></div>既又观陵中之物，见所谓铁罩者，铁几万斤，以木为骨，大不及三寸，其相穿叩之处，厚才寸馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183699_comment'></div>远不过二三十年，决须摧朽，压于梓宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183699_comment'></div>于时私心惶骇，不能自已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183699_comment'></div>使人闻于魏公，魏公不以为意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183699_comment'></div>以魏公之忠孝，于仁皇非不尽心，其蔽于众论，昧于远虑，以天下之力，葬一人于至危之地，可不痛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183699_comment'></div>陵土既覆，固知无可奈何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183699_comment'></div>然每一念之，心悸魄丧，或终夕不寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183699_comment'></div>今乡邻之閒，有如是事，可为谋而不以告人，必谓之不信，况仁皇天下父母乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183699_comment'></div>今也不幸太皇太后奄弃宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183699_comment'></div>因此事会，可为之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183699_comment'></div>夫合葬之礼，周公以来，未之有改，近取诸唐，帝后亦或同穴，至于乾陵，乃是再启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183699_comment'></div>太祖皇帝神谋远虑，超越万古，昭宪太后亦合安陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183699_comment'></div>稽典礼则得尊亲之道，徇俗法则皆享福之永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1183699_comment'></div>此为可行，无足疑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1183699_comment'></div>伏愿公忠诚奋发，为朝廷极论其事，请奉太皇太后合祔昭陵，因得撤去铁罩，用厚陵石椁之制，仍更别加裁处，使异日虽木坏石坠，不能为害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1183699_comment'></div>救仁皇必至之祸，成主上莫大之孝，任此事者，非公孰能？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1183699_comment'></div>诚能为之，天祐忠孝，必俾公炽昌寿臧，子孙保无疆之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1183699_comment'></div>窃惟公事仁宗皇帝三十馀年，位极人臣，恩遇无比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1183699_comment'></div>料公之心，茍能使仁皇圣体保其安全，虽陷祸患，所不避也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1183699_comment'></div>况一言之易，肯顾虑而不发乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1183699_comment'></div>事理至明，顾主上素未知尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1183699_comment'></div>以公言之重，竭诚致恳，再三陈之，不忧朝廷之不悟，独系公为不为尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1183699_comment'></div>哀诚愤激，语辞鄙直，内省狂易，战灼无地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1183699_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1183699_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年</a>　答富公小简。作品：答富郑公小简。<div id='poem_1183700' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183700' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183700?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答富公小简</a><span class='authorDate'>（1079年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183700")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183700_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183700'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183700'>昨日妄有布闻，方怀烦渎之惧，乃辱教诲，加赐酒食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183700_comment'></div>仰荷台意之厚，不胜愧悚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183700_comment'></div>尊者之赐，礼不敢辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183700_comment'></div>然颐方有言于左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183700_comment'></div>公若见取，虽执鞭门下，盖所欣慕，况受赐乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183700_comment'></div>茍不见从，是忘忠义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183700_comment'></div>公之赐也，实为颐羞，未敢拜贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183700_comment'></div>谨复上纳，渎冒台严，第深战慄。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1183700_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年</a>　代富弼上神宗论永昭陵疏。作品：代富郑公上神宗论永昭陵疏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年</a>　吕大临求学于程颐。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
周至（盩厔）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2149966b3b4f4d948b7fd8a425986ec1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2149966b3b4f4d948b7fd8a425986ec1");'><span id='2149966b3b4f4d948b7fd8a425986ec1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年</a>，48岁</div><div id='2149966b3b4f4d948b7fd8a425986ec1' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>至关中，作遗金闲志。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>至关中，上河东帅书。<div id='poem_1183701' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183701' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183701?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上河东帅书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1080年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183701")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183701_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183701'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183701'>颐荷德既深，思报宜异，辄以狂言，浼闻台听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183701_comment'></div>公到镇之初，必多询访。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183701_comment'></div>众人对公之语，颐能料之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183701_comment'></div>当曰：「虏既再寇河外，必不复来，公可高枕矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183701_comment'></div>是常言也，未知奇胜之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183701_comment'></div>兵法曰：「攻必取者，攻其所不守也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183701_comment'></div>谓其不来，乃其所以来也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183701_comment'></div>又曰：「彼兴大众，岂徒然哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183701_comment'></div>河外空矣，复来何利」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183701_comment'></div>是大不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183701_comment'></div>诚使彼得出不意，破荡数垒，足以劳弊一道，为利大矣，何必负载而归，然后为利也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183701_comment'></div>窃恐谋士悦于宽忧，计司幸于缓责，众论既一，公虽未信，而上下之心已懈矣，是可虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183701_comment'></div>宁捐力于不用，毋惜功而致悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183701_comment'></div>莫若使彼闻严备而绝意，则疆埸安矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183701_comment'></div>岂独使敌人知有备而不来？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183701_comment'></div>当使内地之人信可恃而愿往，则一二年閒，便可致完实，长久之策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183701_comment'></div>自古乘塞御敌，必用骁猛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183701_comment'></div>招徕抚养，多在儒将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183701_comment'></div>今日之事则异矣，愿公念之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1183701_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>至关中，答人示奏草书。<div id='poem_1183702' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183702' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183702?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答人示奏草书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1080年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183702")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183702_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183702'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183702'>辱示奏藁，足以见仁人君子爱民之心深切如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183702_comment'></div>钦服！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183702_comment'></div>钦服！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183702_comment'></div>子弟当勉公以速且坚，何可已也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183702_comment'></div>然于愚意有未安者，敢布左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183702_comment'></div>观公之意，专以畏乱为主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183702_comment'></div>颐欲公以爱民为先，力言百姓饥且死，丐朝廷哀怜，因惧将为寇乱可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183702_comment'></div>不惟告君之体当如是，事势亦宜尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183702_comment'></div>公方求财以活人，祈之以仁爱，则当轻财而重民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183702_comment'></div>惧之以利害，则将恃财以自保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183702_comment'></div>古之时得丘民则得天下，财散则人聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183702_comment'></div>后世茍私利于目前，以兵制民，以财聚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183702_comment'></div>聚财者能守，保民者为迂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183702_comment'></div>秦、汉而下，莫不然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183702_comment'></div>窃虑庙堂诸贤，未能免此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183702_comment'></div>惟当以诚意感动，觊其有不忍之心而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183702_comment'></div>浅见无取，惟公裁之！</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1183702_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>赵瞻持丧居周至，以“释氏之学”请教程颐。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>论关中气衰。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
涪陵
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c26f8b2a8b4746a2bcd9e880517a0c5c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c26f8b2a8b4746a2bcd9e880517a0c5c");'><span id='c26f8b2a8b4746a2bcd9e880517a0c5c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1099')">1097-1099年</a>，65-67岁</div><div id='c26f8b2a8b4746a2bcd9e880517a0c5c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年11月</a>　送涪州编管，谢良佐同行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年11月</a>　离开洛阳前往涪州，李邦直送金钱，称已非相知，坚辞不受。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　居涪州，有上谢师直书。作品：上谢帅师直书。<div id='poem_1183714' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183714' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183714?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上谢帅师直书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183714")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183714_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183714'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183714'>颐皇恐上诉于知府安抚宝文阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183714_comment'></div>颐至愚，学道几五十年，惟是自信，行其所知，不敢为世俗所移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183714_comment'></div>知之罪之，则系乎人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183714_comment'></div>伏睹律节文：诸医为人合药，误不如本方杀人者，徒二年半；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183714_comment'></div>故不如本方杀伤人者，以故杀伤论，虽不伤人，杖六十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183714_comment'></div>古人造律之意，非特矜死者之无辜，亦以警惧庸医，使不敢轻妄，致害人命，则其为益，岂不甚大？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183714_comment'></div>近世以来，律虽存而实不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183714_comment'></div>俗吏拘文，乃云律称合药误不如本方，若用药不如方论，虽日杀千人，法所不禁，官不当治也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183714_comment'></div>遂使庸医辈恣其盲妄，无所忌惮，杀人如麻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183714_comment'></div>耳目所闻见，士大夫为庸医反阴阳、背方论而杀之者，不可胜数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183714_comment'></div>况天下之大，民庶之众，可胜言哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183714_comment'></div>独嘉祐中，族兄太中嗣宗知扶沟县，尝以医者用药过剂杀人，送府鞭其背。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183714_comment'></div>过剂乃用医之失，非合药误也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183714_comment'></div>当时众论称之，盖他人未尝用此律故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183714_comment'></div>今死者之家，莫肯与医者辨者，其故有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183714_comment'></div>以当官者无爱人之心，茍欲省事，不肯为之穷辨，一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183714_comment'></div>与医者习熟，不忍讼之，二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1183714_comment'></div>虑今而后，难复用医，三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1183714_comment'></div>是皆以利害为心，而无顾骨肉之义，知其冤死而不为之辨，骨肉之义绝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1183714_comment'></div>既不能辨，则为之词曰彼无恶意，又曰讼之无益矣，又曰己之命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1183714_comment'></div>此皆至愚，不知义理之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1183714_comment'></div>彼有恶意，自当从故杀伤之法，此律正为无故意者设也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1183714_comment'></div>辨之所以申骨肉之义，岂系有益无益也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1183714_comment'></div>谓己之命，则为人殴而杀之，亦可以不校矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1183714_comment'></div>世之人，虽其父母本非死疾，为医所杀，隐忍而不辨者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1183714_comment'></div>众人观之，亦不以为非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1183714_comment'></div>习俗之迷人也如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1183714_comment'></div>今之士大夫，使马医治马，误杀马而杖马医者，目所常见，耳所常闻，众人不以为非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1183714_comment'></div>至以父母骨肉为医所杀而责医者，则未尝见，岂爱亲不若爱马乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1183714_comment'></div>愚惑不思之甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1183714_comment'></div>凡人之疾病，误医者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1183714_comment'></div>若风疾与气药，肝病而攻脾之类，虽不中病，未能害人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1183714_comment'></div>其死乃病死，未得为医杀之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1183714_comment'></div>若医经明言下之则死，是不下则不死也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1183714_comment'></div>今下而杀之，与操刃而断其喉何异？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1183714_comment'></div>古人立法，原其意本不恶，故罪止于徒，恕之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1183714_comment'></div>若听其妄杀人而不加治，岂为政之道乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1183714_comment'></div>侄子某为令醴泉，病阴證伤寒，而邑之医者乃大下之，又与洗心散，遂至冤死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1183714_comment'></div>今有状披诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1183714_comment'></div>伏惟明公居大帅之任，操劝惩之柄，经术政事闻于天下，高识远见卓然绝俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1183714_comment'></div>法之所无者，尚可权其宜而行之，况有法可依者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1183714_comment'></div>民之于令，其义最重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1183714_comment'></div>致令之死，而不加一毫之罪，于义得为安乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1183714_comment'></div>窃闻邑中愤叹不平之声，闻于道路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1183714_comment'></div>岂当任者独不念之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1183714_comment'></div>重思阁下，天下吏师，诚能行之，郡县必多效之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1183714_comment'></div>若使远近传之，庸医之辈皆知戒惧，不敢轻视人命，则公及人之功，岂细也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1183714_comment'></div>匪惟先兄父子怀结草之报，当获上天之祐，后昆享繁衍盛大之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1183714_comment'></div>不胜哀恳，颐皇恐上诉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1183714_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　居涪州，作文祭侄儿程端本。作品：祭四十一郎文。<div id='poem_1183795' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183795' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183795?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭四十一郎文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183795")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183795_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183795'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183795'>叔父颐令昂具酒肴致祭于侄四十一郎之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183795_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183795_comment'></div>乃祖乃父，世积庆善，而汝兄弟姊妹皆不克寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183795_comment'></div>天造差忒，至如是乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183795_comment'></div>惟汝资禀善和修谨，无子弟之过，期汝有成，而遽死耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183795_comment'></div>吾方以罪戾，窜絷远方，生不获视汝疾，死不获抚汝柩，冤痛之深，衷肠如割。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183795_comment'></div>吾知汝有未伸之志，抱无穷之恨，吾当致力，慰尔心于泉下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183795_comment'></div>又汝妇盛年，自今当待之加厚，冀其安室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183795_comment'></div>嗣子循良，今已可见，当教诲之，期于成立，则汝为有后矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183795_comment'></div>此外吾无以致其力矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183795_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183795_comment'></div>吾将七十，望汝收我，而我反哭汝，天乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183795_comment'></div>冤哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1183795_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　居涪州，有书信与谢湜。作品：与金堂谢君书。<div id='poem_1183715' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183715' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183715?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与金堂谢君书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183715")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183715_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183715'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183715'>颐启：前月末，吴斋郎送到书信，即递中奉报，计半月方达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183715_comment'></div>冬寒，远想雅履安和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183715_comment'></div>侨居旋为客次，日以延望，乃知止行，甚悒悒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183715_comment'></div>来春江水稳善，候有所授，能一访甚佳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183715_comment'></div>只云忠涪閒看亲，人必不疑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183715_comment'></div>颐偕小子甚安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183715_comment'></div>来春本欲作《春秋》文字，以此无书，故未能，却先了《论》、《孟》或《礼记》也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183715_comment'></div>《春秋》大义数十，皎如日星，不容遗忘，只恐微细义例，老年精神有所漏落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183715_comment'></div>且请推官用意寻究，后日见助，如往年所说，许止、蔡般书葬类是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183715_comment'></div>若欲治《易》，先寻绎令熟，只看王弼、胡先生、王介甫三家文字，令通贯，馀人《易》说无取，枉费功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183715_comment'></div>年亦长矣，宜汲汲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183715_comment'></div>未相见閒，千百慎爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183715_comment'></div>十一月初九日，颐启。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1183715_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年1月</a>　居涪，《易傅》成，作序。作品：周易传序。<div id='poem_1183734' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1183734' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1183734?labeling=true' target='_blank'>易传序</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29922, "北宋", "程颐", "poem_title_1183734")'>程颐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1183734_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1183734'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1183734'>《易》，变易也，随时变易以从道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1183734_comment'></div>其为书也，广大悉备，将以顺性命之理，通幽明之故，尽事物之情，而示开物成务之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1183734_comment'></div>圣人之忧患后世，可谓至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1183734_comment'></div>去古虽远，遗经尚存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1183734_comment'></div>然而前儒失意以传言，后学诵言而忘味，自秦而下，盖无传矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1183734_comment'></div>予生千载之后，悼斯文之湮晦，将俾后人沿流而求源，此《传》所以作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1183734_comment'></div>《易》有圣人之道四焉：以言者尚其辞，以动者尚其变，以制器者尚其象，以卜筮者尚其占。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1183734_comment'></div>吉凶消长之理，进退存亡之道，备于辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1183734_comment'></div>推辞考卦，可以知变，象与占在其中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1183734_comment'></div>君子居则观其象而玩其辞，动则观其变而玩其占。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1183734_comment'></div>得于辞，不达其意者有矣，未有不得于辞而能通其意者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1183734_comment'></div>至微者理也，至著者象也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1183734_comment'></div>体用一源，显微无间，观会通以行其典礼，则辞无所不备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1183734_comment'></div>故善学者，求言必自近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1183734_comment'></div>易于近者，非知言者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1183734_comment'></div>予所传者辞也，由辞以得意，则在乎人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1183734_comment'></div>有宋元符二年己卯正月庚申，河南程颐正叔谨序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1183734_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>　以《易》传示门人，郭忠孝、尹焞等人论《易传序》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>　与谯定游泳北山之岩。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>　称赞范祖禹“其人如玉”<br /></div>
-----end
